I've uploaded a code repository in the directory . Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[BUG] S3 CopyObject returns NoSuchKey for objects with non-ASCII (multibyte) keys

## Service

S3

## AWS API Action

CopyObject

## Expected behavior

`CopyObject` should succeed when the source key contains non-ASCII characters (e.g. Japanese/CJK), since `PutObject` and `GetObject` work correctly with the same key.

## Actual behavior

`CopyObject` returns `NoSuchKey: The specified key does not exist.` when the `CopySource` key contains multibyte characters, even though the object exists and can be retrieved via `GetObject`.

## Reproduction

```python
import boto3

s3 = boto3.client('s3', endpoint_url='http://localhost:4566',
                  region_name='ap-northeast-1',
                  aws_access_key_id='test', aws_secret_access_key='test')

s3.create_bucket(Bucket='test-bucket',
                 CreateBucketConfiguration={'LocationConstraint': 'ap-northeast-1'})

# PutObject with Japanese key — succeeds
s3.put_object(Bucket='test-bucket', Key='src/テスト画像.png', Body=b'hello')

# GetObject — succeeds
resp = s3.get_object(Bucket='test-bucket', Key='src/テスト画像.png')
print(resp['Body'].read())  # b'hello'

# CopyObject — fails with NoSuchKey
s3.copy_object(
    Bucket='test-bucket',
    Key='dst/テスト画像.png',
    CopySource={'Bucket': 'test-bucket', 'Key': 'src/テスト画像.png'}
)
# botocore.errorfactory.NoSuchKey: An error occurred (NoSuchKey) when calling the CopyObject operation
```

Note: `CopyObject` with ASCII-only keys works correctly.

## Environment

- Floci version / image tag: `hectorvent/floci:latest` (1.0.11)
- How you're running Floci: Docker


</pr_description>

    78	    private S3Service(StorageBackend<String, Bucket> bucketStore,
    79	                      StorageBackend<String, S3Object> objectStore,
    80	                      Path dataRoot, boolean inMemory, SqsService sqsService, SnsService snsService,
    81	                      RegionResolver regionResolver, String baseUrl, ObjectMapper objectMapper) {
    82	        this.bucketStore = bucketStore;
    83	        this.objectStore = objectStore;
    84	        this.dataRoot = dataRoot;
    85	        this.inMemory = inMemory;
    86	        this.sqsService = sqsService;
    87	        this.snsService = snsService;
    88	        this.regionResolver = regionResolver;
    89	        this.baseUrl = baseUrl;
    90	        this.objectMapper = objectMapper;
    91	        if (!inMemory) {
    92	            try {
    93	                Files.createDirectories(dataRoot);
    94	            } catch (IOException e) {
    95	                throw new UncheckedIOException("Failed to create S3 data directory: " + dataRoot, e);
    96	            }
    97	        }

   100	    public Bucket createBucket(String bucketName, String region) {
   101	        var existing = bucketStore.get(bucketName);
   102	        if (existing.isPresent()) {
   103	            throw new AwsException("BucketAlreadyOwnedByYou",
   104	                    "Your previous request to create the named bucket succeeded and you already own it.", 409);
   105	        }
   106	
   107	        Bucket bucket = new Bucket(bucketName);
   108	        bucket.setRegion(region);
   109	        bucketStore.put(bucketName, bucket);
   110	        LOG.infov("Created bucket: {0} in region: {1}", bucketName, region);
   111	        return bucket;
   112	    }
   113	
   114	    public void deleteBucket(String bucketName) {
   115	        ensureBucketExists(bucketName);
   116	
   117	        // Check if bucket is empty
   118	        List<S3Object> objects = listObjects(bucketName, null, null, 1);
   119	        if (!objects.isEmpty()) {
   120	            throw new AwsException("BucketNotEmpty",
   121	                    "The bucket you tried to delete is not empty.", 409);
   122	        }
   123	
   124	        bucketStore.delete(bucketName);
   125	        if (inMemory) {
   126	            String prefix = bucketName + "/";
   127	            memoryDataStore.keySet().removeIf(k -> k.startsWith(prefix));
   128	        } else {
   129	            deleteDirectory(dataRoot.resolve(bucketName));
   130	        }
   131	        LOG.infov("Deleted bucket: {0}", bucketName);
   132	    }

   149	
   150	    public S3Object putObject(String bucketName, String key, byte[] data,
   151	                              String contentType, Map<String, String> metadata, String storageClass,
   152	                              String objectLockMode, Instant retainUntilDate, String legalHoldStatus) {
   153	        S3Object object = storeObject(bucketName, key, data, contentType, metadata, storageClass, null, null,
   154	                objectLockMode, retainUntilDate, legalHoldStatus);
   155	        fireNotifications(bucketName, key, "ObjectCreated:Put", object);
   156	        return object;
   157	    }
   158	
   159	    /**
   160	     * Store object without firing notifications (used internally by completeMultipartUpload).
   161	     */
   162	    private S3Object storeObject(String bucketName, String key, byte[] data,
   163	                                 String contentType, Map<String, String> metadata) {
   164	        return storeObject(bucketName, key, data, contentType, metadata, null, null, null,
   165	                null, null, null);
   166	    }
   167	
   168	    private S3Object storeObject(String bucketName, String key, byte[] data,
   169	                                 String contentType, Map<String, String> metadata, String storageClass,
   170	                                 S3Checksum checksum, List<Part> parts,
   171	                                 String objectLockMode, Instant retainUntilDate, String legalHoldStatus) {
   172	        Bucket bucket = bucketStore.get(bucketName)
   173	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NoSuchBucket",
   174	                        "The specified bucket does not exist.", 404));
   175	
   176	        S3Object object = new S3Object(bucketName, key, data, contentType);
   177	        if (metadata != null) {
   178	            object.getMetadata().putAll(metadata);
   179	        }
   180	        object.setStorageClass(ObjectAttributeName.normalizeStorageClass(storageClass));
   181	        object.setChecksum(checksum != null ? copyChecksum(checksum) : buildChecksum(data, parts, false));
   182	        object.setParts(copyParts(parts));
   183	
   184	        if (bucket.isVersioningEnabled()) {
   185	            String versionId = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
   186	            object.setVersionId(versionId);
   187	            object.setLatest(true);
   188	
   189	            // Check lock protection on the current latest before overwriting
   190	            String latestKey = objectKey(bucketName, key);
   191	            objectStore.get(latestKey).ifPresent(prev -> {
   192	                if (prev.isLatest() && !prev.isDeleteMarker() && bucket.isObjectLockEnabled()) {
   193	                    checkLockProtection(prev, false);
   194	                }
   195	                if (prev.getVersionId() != null) {
   196	                    prev.setLatest(false);
   197	                    objectStore.put(versionedKey(bucketName, key, prev.getVersionId()), prev);
   198	                }
   199	            });
   200	
   201	            // Apply lock fields from request or bucket default
   202	            applyObjectLock(object, bucket, objectLockMode, retainUntilDate, legalHoldStatus);
   203	
   204	            // Store versioned copy and update latest pointer
   205	            objectStore.put(versionedKey(bucketName, key, versionId), object);
   206	            objectStore.put(latestKey, object);
   207	            writeFile(bucketName, key, data);
   208	            writeVersionedFile(bucketName, key, versionId, data);
   209	            LOG.debugv("Put versioned object: {0}/{1} v={2} ({3} bytes)", bucketName, key, versionId, data.length);
   210	        } else {
   211	            // Check lock protection on the existing object before overwriting
   212	            if (bucket.isObjectLockEnabled()) {
   213	                objectStore.get(objectKey(bucketName, key)).ifPresent(prev -> {
   214	                    if (!prev.isDeleteMarker()) {
   215	                        checkLockProtection(prev, false);
   216	                    }
   217	                });
   218	            }
   219	
   220	            // Apply lock fields from request or bucket default
   221	            applyObjectLock(object, bucket, objectLockMode, retainUntilDate, legalHoldStatus);
   222	
   223	            objectStore.put(objectKey(bucketName, key), object);
   224	            writeFile(bucketName, key, data);
   225	            LOG.debugv("Put object: {0}/{1} ({2} bytes)", bucketName, key, data.length);
   226	        }
   227	        return object;
   228	    }
   229	
   230	    private void applyObjectLock(S3Object object, Bucket bucket,
   231	                                 String objectLockMode, Instant retainUntilDate, String legalHoldStatus) {
   232	        if (objectLockMode != null) {
   233	            object.setObjectLockMode(objectLockMode);
   234	            object.setRetainUntilDate(retainUntilDate);
   235	        } else if (bucket.isObjectLockEnabled() && bucket.getDefaultRetention() != null) {
   236	            ObjectLockRetention def = bucket.getDefaultRetention();
   237	            object.setObjectLockMode(def.mode());
   238	            long days = "Years".equals(def.unit()) ? (long) def.value() * 365 : def.value();
   239	            object.setRetainUntilDate(Instant.now().plusSeconds(days * 86400L));
   240	        }
   241	        if (legalHoldStatus != null) {
   242	            object.setLegalHoldStatus(legalHoldStatus);
   243	        }
   244	    }
   245	
   246	    private void checkLockProtection(S3Object obj, boolean bypassGovernance) {
   247	        if ("ON".equals(obj.getLegalHoldStatus())) {
   248	            throw new AwsException("AccessDenied", "Object has an active legal hold", 403);
   249	        }
   250	        if (obj.getRetainUntilDate() != null && Instant.now().isBefore(obj.getRetainUntilDate())) {
   251	            if ("COMPLIANCE".equals(obj.getObjectLockMode())) {
   252	                throw new AwsException("AccessDenied", "Object is protected by COMPLIANCE retention", 403);
   253	            }
   254	            if ("GOVERNANCE".equals(obj.getObjectLockMode()) && !bypassGovernance) {
   255	                throw new AwsException("AccessDenied", "Object is protected by GOVERNANCE retention", 403);
   256	            }
   257	        }
   258	    }

   264	    public S3Object getObject(String bucketName, String key, String versionId) {
   265	        S3Object obj = getObjectMetadata(bucketName, key, versionId);
   266	
   267	        // Read from versioned file if available, otherwise from latest
   268	        if (versionId != null) {
   269	            obj.setData(readVersionedFile(bucketName, key, versionId));
   270	        } else {
   271	            obj.setData(readFile(bucketName, key));
   272	        }
   273	        return obj;
   274	    }

   284	    public S3Object getObjectMetadata(String bucketName, String key, String versionId) {
   285	        S3Object copy = copyObject(getStoredObject(bucketName, key, versionId));
   286	        copy.setData(null);
   287	        return copy;
   288	    }
   289	
   290	    public GetObjectAttributesResult getObjectAttributes(String bucketName, String key, String versionId,
   291	                                                         Set<ObjectAttributeName> attributes,
   292	                                                         Integer maxParts, Integer partNumberMarker) {
   293	        S3Object object = getObjectMetadata(bucketName, key, versionId);
   294	
   295	        GetObjectAttributesResult result = new GetObjectAttributesResult();
   296	        result.setLastModified(object.getLastModified());
   297	        result.setVersionId(object.getVersionId());
   298	
   299	        if (attributes.contains(ObjectAttributeName.E_TAG)) {
   300	            result.setETag(object.getETag());
   301	        }
   302	        if (attributes.contains(ObjectAttributeName.STORAGE_CLASS)) {
   303	            result.setStorageClass(object.getStorageClass());
   304	        }
   305	        if (attributes.contains(ObjectAttributeName.OBJECT_SIZE)) {
   306	            result.setObjectSize(object.getSize());
   307	        }
   308	        if (attributes.contains(ObjectAttributeName.CHECKSUM)) {
   309	            result.setChecksum(copyChecksum(object.getChecksum()));
   310	        }
   311	        if (attributes.contains(ObjectAttributeName.OBJECT_PARTS)) {
   312	            result.setObjectParts(buildObjectParts(object, maxParts, partNumberMarker));
   313	        }
   314	
   315	        return result;
   316	    }
   317	
   318	    private S3Object getStoredObject(String bucketName, String key, String versionId) {
   319	        ensureBucketExists(bucketName);
   320	
   321	        String storeKey = versionId != null ? versionedKey(bucketName, key, versionId) : objectKey(bucketName, key);
   322	        S3Object object = objectStore.get(storeKey)
   323	                .orElseThrow(() -> versionId != null
   324	                        ? new AwsException("NoSuchVersion", "The specified version does not exist.", 404)
   325	                        : new AwsException("NoSuchKey", "The specified key does not exist.", 404));
   326	        if (object.isDeleteMarker()) {
   327	            throw new AwsException("NoSuchKey", "The specified key does not exist.", 404);
   328	        }
   329	        return object;
   330	    }
   331	
   332	    private GetObjectAttributesParts buildObjectParts(S3Object object, Integer maxParts, Integer partNumberMarker) {
   333	        List<Part> sortedParts = new ArrayList<>(copyParts(object.getParts()));
   334	        sortedParts.sort(Comparator.comparingInt(Part::getPartNumber));
   335	
   336	        int max = (maxParts == null || maxParts <= 0) ? 1000 : maxParts;
   337	        int marker = Math.max(partNumberMarker != null ? partNumberMarker : 0, 0);
   338	
   339	        List<Part> visibleParts = sortedParts.stream()
   340	                .filter(part -> part.getPartNumber() > marker)
   341	                .toList();
   342	        List<Part> returnedParts = visibleParts.stream().limit(max).toList();
   343	
   344	        GetObjectAttributesParts result = new GetObjectAttributesParts();
   345	        result.setMaxParts(max);
   346	        result.setPartNumberMarker(marker);
   347	        result.setParts(returnedParts);
   348	        result.setPartsCount(sortedParts.size());
   349	        result.setTruncated(visibleParts.size() > returnedParts.size());
   350	        result.setNextPartNumberMarker(returnedParts.isEmpty()
   351	                ? marker
   352	                : returnedParts.get(returnedParts.size() - 1).getPartNumber());
   353	        return result;
   354	    }

   356	    public S3Object deleteObject(String bucketName, String key) {
   357	        return deleteObject(bucketName, key, null, false);
   358	    }

   360	    public S3Object deleteObject(String bucketName, String key, String versionId) {
   361	        return deleteObject(bucketName, key, versionId, false);
   362	    }
   363	
   364	    public S3Object deleteObject(String bucketName, String key, String versionId, boolean bypassGovernance) {
   365	        Bucket bucket = bucketStore.get(bucketName)
   366	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NoSuchBucket",
   367	                        "The specified bucket does not exist.", 404));
   368	
   369	        if (bucket.isVersioningEnabled() && versionId == null) {
   370	            // Check lock on current latest before placing a delete marker
   371	            objectStore.get(objectKey(bucketName, key)).ifPresent(prev -> {
   372	                if (!prev.isDeleteMarker()) {
   373	                    checkLockProtection(prev, bypassGovernance);
   374	                }
   375	            });
   376	
   377	            // Create a delete marker instead of actually deleting
   378	            S3Object deleteMarker = new S3Object(bucketName, key, new byte[0], null);
   379	            String markerId = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
   380	            deleteMarker.setVersionId(markerId);
   381	            deleteMarker.setDeleteMarker(true);
   382	            deleteMarker.setLatest(true);
   383	
   384	            // Mark previous latest as not latest
   385	            objectStore.get(objectKey(bucketName, key)).ifPresent(prev -> {
   386	                if (prev.getVersionId() != null) {
   387	                    prev.setLatest(false);
   388	                    objectStore.put(versionedKey(bucketName, key, prev.getVersionId()), prev);
   389	                }
   390	            });
   391	
   392	            objectStore.put(versionedKey(bucketName, key, markerId), deleteMarker);
   393	            objectStore.put(objectKey(bucketName, key), deleteMarker);
   394	            LOG.debugv("Created delete marker: {0}/{1} v={2}", bucketName, key, markerId);
   395	            fireNotifications(bucketName, key, "ObjectRemoved:DeleteMarkerCreated", deleteMarker);
   396	            return deleteMarker;
   397	        } else if (versionId != null) {
   398	            // Check lock on the specific version before permanent deletion
   399	            objectStore.get(versionedKey(bucketName, key, versionId)).ifPresent(obj -> {
   400	                if (!obj.isDeleteMarker()) {
   401	                    checkLockProtection(obj, bypassGovernance);
   402	                }
   403	            });
   404	            // Permanently delete a specific version
   405	            objectStore.delete(versionedKey(bucketName, key, versionId));
   406	            LOG.debugv("Permanently deleted version: {0}/{1} v={2}", bucketName, key, versionId);
   407	            return null;
   408	        } else {
   409	            // Check lock on the non-versioned object before delete
   410	            objectStore.get(objectKey(bucketName, key)).ifPresent(obj -> {
   411	                if (!obj.isDeleteMarker()) {
   412	                    checkLockProtection(obj, bypassGovernance);
   413	                }
   414	            });
   415	            // Non-versioned delete
   416	            objectStore.delete(objectKey(bucketName, key));
   417	            deleteFile(bucketName, key);
   418	            LOG.debugv("Deleted object: {0}/{1}", bucketName, key);
   419	            fireNotifications(bucketName, key, "ObjectRemoved:Delete", null);
   420	            return null;
   421	        }
   422	    }
   423	
   424	    public List<S3Object> listObjects(String bucketName, String prefix, String delimiter, int maxKeys) {
   425	        ensureBucketExists(bucketName);
   426	
   427	        String keyPrefix = bucketName + "/";
   428	        String fullPrefix = prefix != null ? keyPrefix + prefix : keyPrefix;
   429	
   430	        // Filter out versioned entries (contain #v#) and delete markers
   431	        List<S3Object> allObjects = objectStore.scan(key ->
   432	                        key.startsWith(fullPrefix) && !key.contains("#v#"))
   433	                .stream()
   434	                .filter(obj -> !obj.isDeleteMarker())
   435	                .toList();
   436	        allObjects = new ArrayList<>(allObjects);
   437	
   438	        if (delimiter != null && !delimiter.isEmpty()) {
   439	            // Filter to only return objects at this level (simulate directory listing)
   440	            allObjects = allObjects.stream()
   441	                    .filter(obj -> {
   442	                        String remainder = obj.getKey().substring(prefix != null ? prefix.length() : 0);
   443	                        return !remainder.contains(delimiter);
   444	                    })
   445	                    .toList();
   446	        }
   447	
   448	        if (maxKeys > 0 && allObjects.size() > maxKeys) {
   449	            allObjects = allObjects.subList(0, maxKeys);
   450	        }
   451	
   452	        return allObjects;
   453	    }
   454	
   455	    public S3Object copyObject(String sourceBucket, String sourceKey,
   456	                               String destBucket, String destKey) {
   457	        return copyObject(sourceBucket, sourceKey, destBucket, destKey,
   458	                null, null, null, null);
   459	    }
   460	
   461	    public S3Object copyObject(String sourceBucket, String sourceKey,
   462	                               String destBucket, String destKey,
   463	                               String metadataDirective, Map<String, String> replacementMetadata,
   464	                               String storageClass, String contentType) {
   465	        S3Object source = getObject(sourceBucket, sourceKey);
   466	        ensureBucketExists(destBucket);
   467	
   468	        boolean replaceMetadata = "REPLACE".equalsIgnoreCase(metadataDirective);
   469	        Map<String, String> metadata = replaceMetadata ? new LinkedHashMap<>() : new LinkedHashMap<>(source.getMetadata());
   470	        if (replaceMetadata && replacementMetadata != null) {
   471	            metadata.putAll(replacementMetadata);
   472	        }
   473	
   474	        String effectiveContentType = replaceMetadata && contentType != null ? contentType : source.getContentType();
   475	        String effectiveStorageClass = storageClass != null ? storageClass : source.getStorageClass();
   476	        S3Object copy = storeObject(destBucket, destKey, source.getData(), effectiveContentType, metadata,
   477	                effectiveStorageClass, source.getChecksum(), source.getParts(), null, null, null);
   478	        copy.setETag(source.getETag());
   479	        LOG.debugv("Copied object: {0}/{1} -> {2}/{3}", sourceBucket, sourceKey, destBucket, destKey);
   480	        fireNotifications(destBucket, destKey, "ObjectCreated:Copy", copy);
   481	        return copy;
   482	    }
   483	
   484	    // --- Versioning Operations ---
   485	
   486	    public void putBucketVersioning(String bucketName, String status) {
   487	        Bucket bucket = bucketStore.get(bucketName)
   488	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NoSuchBucket",
   489	                        "The specified bucket does not exist.", 404));
   490	        if (!"Enabled".equals(status) && !"Suspended".equals(status)) {
   491	            throw new AwsException("MalformedXML",
   492	                    "Versioning status must be 'Enabled' or 'Suspended'.", 400);
   493	        }
   494	        bucket.setVersioningStatus(status);
   495	        bucketStore.put(bucketName, bucket);
   496	        LOG.infov("Set versioning for bucket {0}: {1}", bucketName, status);
   497	    }
   498	
   499	    public String getBucketVersioning(String bucketName) {
   500	        Bucket bucket = bucketStore.get(bucketName)
   501	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NoSuchBucket",
   502	                        "The specified bucket does not exist.", 404));
   503	        return bucket.getVersioningStatus();
   504	    }
   505	
   506	    public List<S3Object> listObjectVersions(String bucketName, String prefix, int maxKeys) {
   507	        ensureBucketExists(bucketName);
   508	
   509	        String versionPrefix = bucketName + "/";
   510	        String fullPrefix = prefix != null ? versionPrefix + prefix : versionPrefix;
   511	
   512	        // Scan for versioned entries (contain #v#)
   513	        List<S3Object> versions = new ArrayList<>(objectStore.scan(key ->
   514	                key.startsWith(fullPrefix) && key.contains("#v#")));
   515	
   516	        // Sort by key, then by lastModified descending
   517	        versions.sort((a, b) -> {
   518	            int keyCompare = a.getKey().compareTo(b.getKey());
   519	            if (keyCompare != 0) return keyCompare;
   520	            return b.getLastModified().compareTo(a.getLastModified());
   521	        });
   522	
   523	        if (maxKeys > 0 && versions.size() > maxKeys) {
   524	            versions = versions.subList(0, maxKeys);
   525	        }
   526	        return versions;
   527	    }

   540	    // --- Batch Delete ---
   541	
   542	    public record DeleteResult(String key, String versionId, boolean deleteMarker, String deleteMarkerVersionId) {
   543	    }
   544	
   545	    public record DeleteError(String key, String code, String message) {
   546	    }
   547	
   548	    public record DeleteObjectsResult(List<DeleteResult> deleted, List<DeleteError> errors) {
   549	    }
   550	
   551	    public DeleteObjectsResult deleteObjects(String bucketName, List<String> keys) {
   552	        ensureBucketExists(bucketName);
   553	        List<DeleteResult> deleted = new ArrayList<>();
   554	        List<DeleteError> errors = new ArrayList<>();
   555	        for (String key : keys) {
   556	            try {
   557	                S3Object result = deleteObject(bucketName, key);
   558	                if (result != null && result.isDeleteMarker()) {
   559	                    deleted.add(new DeleteResult(key, null, true, result.getVersionId()));
   560	                } else {
   561	                    deleted.add(new DeleteResult(key, null, false, null));
   562	                }
   563	            } catch (Exception e) {
   564	                errors.add(new DeleteError(key, "InternalError", e.getMessage()));
   565	            }
   566	        }
   567	        return new DeleteObjectsResult(deleted, errors);
   568	    }

   638	    public void putObjectLockConfiguration(String bucketName, String mode, String unit, int value) {
   639	        Bucket bucket = bucketStore.get(bucketName)
   640	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NoSuchBucket",
   641	                        "The specified bucket does not exist.", 404));
   642	        bucket.setBucketObjectLockEnabled();
   643	        if (mode != null && unit != null && value > 0) {
   644	            bucket.setDefaultRetention(new ObjectLockRetention(mode, unit, value));
   645	        } else {
   646	            bucket.setDefaultRetention(null);
   647	        }
   648	        bucketStore.put(bucketName, bucket);
   649	        LOG.infov("Set Object Lock configuration for bucket: {0}, mode={1}, unit={2}, value={3}",
   650	                bucketName, mode, unit, value);
   651	    }
   652	
   653	    public ObjectLockRetention getObjectLockConfiguration(String bucketName) {
   654	        Bucket bucket = bucketStore.get(bucketName)
   655	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NoSuchBucket",
   656	                        "The specified bucket does not exist.", 404));
   657	        return bucket.getDefaultRetention();
   658	    }
   659	
   660	    public void putObjectRetention(String bucketName, String key, String versionId,
   661	                                   String mode, Instant retainUntil, boolean bypassGovernance) {
   662	        ensureBucketExists(bucketName);
   663	        String storeKey = versionId != null
   664	                ? versionedKey(bucketName, key, versionId)
   665	                : objectKey(bucketName, key);
   666	        S3Object obj = objectStore.get(storeKey)
   667	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NoSuchKey",
   668	                        "The specified key does not exist.", 404));
   669	
   670	        // COMPLIANCE mode: retainUntil cannot be shortened
   671	        if ("COMPLIANCE".equals(obj.getObjectLockMode())
   672	                && obj.getRetainUntilDate() != null
   673	                && retainUntil != null
   674	                && retainUntil.isBefore(obj.getRetainUntilDate())) {
   675	            throw new AwsException("AccessDenied",
   676	                    "COMPLIANCE retention period cannot be shortened", 403);
   677	        }
   678	
   679	        // Check bypass permission for existing governance lock when shortening/removing
   680	        if ("GOVERNANCE".equals(obj.getObjectLockMode())
   681	                && obj.getRetainUntilDate() != null
   682	                && Instant.now().isBefore(obj.getRetainUntilDate())
   683	                && !bypassGovernance) {
   684	            if (retainUntil == null || retainUntil.isBefore(obj.getRetainUntilDate())) {
   685	                throw new AwsException("AccessDenied",
   686	                        "Object is protected by GOVERNANCE retention", 403);
   687	            }
   688	        }
   689	
   690	        obj.setObjectLockMode(mode);
   691	        obj.setRetainUntilDate(retainUntil);
   692	        objectStore.put(storeKey, obj);
   693	        LOG.debugv("Set retention on {0}/{1}: mode={2}, until={3}", bucketName, key, mode, retainUntil);
   694	    }
   695	
   696	    public S3Object getObjectRetention(String bucketName, String key, String versionId) {
   697	        ensureBucketExists(bucketName);
   698	        String storeKey = versionId != null
   699	                ? versionedKey(bucketName, key, versionId)
   700	                : objectKey(bucketName, key);
   701	        return objectStore.get(storeKey)
   702	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NoSuchKey",
   703	                        "The specified key does not exist.", 404));
   704	    }

   729	    // --- Multipart Upload Operations ---
   730	
   731	    public MultipartUpload initiateMultipartUpload(String bucket, String key, String contentType) {
   732	        return initiateMultipartUpload(bucket, key, contentType, null, null);
   733	    }
   734	
   735	    public MultipartUpload initiateMultipartUpload(String bucket, String key, String contentType,
   736	                                                   Map<String, String> metadata, String storageClass) {
   737	        ensureBucketExists(bucket);
   738	        MultipartUpload upload = new MultipartUpload(bucket, key, contentType);
   739	        if (metadata != null) {
   740	            upload.getMetadata().putAll(metadata);
   741	        }
   742	        upload.setStorageClass(ObjectAttributeName.normalizeStorageClass(storageClass));
   743	
   744	        if (inMemory) {
   745	            memoryMultipartStore.put(upload.getUploadId(), new ConcurrentHashMap<>());
   746	        } else {
   747	            try {
   748	                Files.createDirectories(dataRoot.resolve(".multipart").resolve(upload.getUploadId()));
   749	            } catch (IOException e) {
   750	                throw new UncheckedIOException("Failed to create multipart temp directory", e);
   751	            }
   752	        }
   753	
   754	        multipartUploads.put(upload.getUploadId(), upload);
   755	        LOG.infov("Initiated multipart upload: {0}/{1}, uploadId={2}", bucket, key, upload.getUploadId());
   756	        return upload;
   757	    }
   758	
   759	    public String uploadPart(String bucket, String key, String uploadId, int partNumber, byte[] data) {
   760	        MultipartUpload upload = multipartUploads.get(uploadId);
   761	        if (upload == null || !upload.getBucket().equals(bucket) || !upload.getKey().equals(key)) {
   762	            throw new AwsException("NoSuchUpload",
   763	                    "The specified multipart upload does not exist.", 404);
   764	        }
   765	        if (partNumber < 1 || partNumber > 10000) {
   766	            throw new AwsException("InvalidArgument",
   767	                    "Part number must be between 1 and 10000.", 400);
   768	        }
   769	
   770	        if (inMemory) {
   771	            memoryMultipartStore.get(uploadId).put(partNumber, data);
   772	        } else {
   773	            Path partPath = dataRoot.resolve(".multipart").resolve(uploadId).resolve(String.valueOf(partNumber));
   774	            try {
   775	                Files.write(partPath, data);
   776	            } catch (IOException e) {
   777	                throw new UncheckedIOException("Failed to write multipart part", e);
   778	            }
   779	        }
   780	
   781	        String eTag = computeETag(data);
   782	        Part part = new Part(partNumber, eTag, data.length);
   783	        part.setChecksum(buildChecksum(data, List.of(part), true));
   784	        upload.getParts().put(partNumber, part);
   785	        LOG.debugv("Uploaded part {0} for upload {1} ({2} bytes)", partNumber, uploadId, data.length);
   786	        return eTag;
   787	    }
   788	
   789	    public S3Object completeMultipartUpload(String bucket, String key, String uploadId, List<Integer> partNumbers) {
   790	        MultipartUpload upload = multipartUploads.get(uploadId);
   791	        if (upload == null || !upload.getBucket().equals(bucket) || !upload.getKey().equals(key)) {
   792	            throw new AwsException("NoSuchUpload",
   793	                    "The specified multipart upload does not exist.", 404);
   794	        }
   795	
   796	        // Verify all requested parts exist
   797	        for (int num : partNumbers) {
   798	            if (!upload.getParts().containsKey(num)) {
   799	                throw new AwsException("InvalidPart",
   800	                        "One or more of the specified parts could not be found. Part " + num + " is missing.", 400);
   801	            }
   802	        }
   803	
   804	        // Concatenate parts in order
   805	        try {
   806	            ByteArrayOutputStream combined = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
   807	            MessageDigest md = MessageDigest.getInstance("MD5");
   808	
   809	            for (int num : partNumbers) {
   810	                byte[] partData = inMemory
   811	                        ? memoryMultipartStore.get(uploadId).get(num)
   812	                        : Files.readAllBytes(dataRoot.resolve(".multipart").resolve(uploadId).resolve(String.valueOf(num)));
   813	                combined.write(partData);
   814	                // For composite ETag: hash each part's MD5
   815	                md.update(computeETagBytes(partData));
   816	            }
   817	
   818	            byte[] allData = combined.toByteArray();
   819	
   820	            // Composite ETag: MD5 of concatenated part MD5s, suffixed with part count
   821	            String compositeETag = "\"" + bytesToHex(md.digest()) + "-" + partNumbers.size() + "\"";
   822	
   823	            List<Part> completedParts = partNumbers.stream()
   824	                    .map(num -> copyPart(upload.getParts().get(num)))
   825	                    .toList();
   826	            S3Checksum checksum = buildChecksum(allData, completedParts, true);
   827	            S3Object object = storeObject(bucket, key, allData, upload.getContentType(), upload.getMetadata(),
   828	                    upload.getStorageClass(), checksum, completedParts, null, null, null);
   829	            // Override the ETag with the composite multipart ETag
   830	            object.setETag(compositeETag);
   831	            objectStore.put(objectKey(bucket, key), object);
   832	
   833	            // Cleanup
   834	            cleanupMultipart(uploadId);
   835	            LOG.infov("Completed multipart upload: {0}/{1}, uploadId={2}, parts={3}",
   836	                    bucket, key, uploadId, partNumbers.size());
   837	            fireNotifications(bucket, key, "ObjectCreated:CompleteMultipartUpload", object);
   838	            return object;
   839	        } catch (IOException e) {
   840	            throw new UncheckedIOException("Failed to read multipart parts", e);
   841	        } catch (NoSuchAlgorithmException e) {
   842	            throw new RuntimeException("MD5 algorithm not available", e);
   843	        }
   844	    }
   845	
   846	    public void abortMultipartUpload(String bucket, String key, String uploadId) {
   847	        MultipartUpload upload = multipartUploads.get(uploadId);
   848	        if (upload == null || !upload.getBucket().equals(bucket) || !upload.getKey().equals(key)) {
   849	            throw new AwsException("NoSuchUpload",
   850	                    "The specified multipart upload does not exist.", 404);
   851	        }
   852	        cleanupMultipart(uploadId);
   853	        LOG.infov("Aborted multipart upload: {0}/{1}, uploadId={2}", bucket, key, uploadId);
   854	    }
   855	
   856	    public List<MultipartUpload> listMultipartUploads(String bucket) {
   857	        ensureBucketExists(bucket);
   858	        return multipartUploads.values().stream()
   859	                .filter(u -> u.getBucket().equals(bucket))
   860	                .toList();
   861	    }

  1008	    private String defaultAclXml(String id, String displayName) {
  1009	        return new XmlBuilder()
  1010	                .start("AccessControlPolicy")
  1011	                  .start("Owner")
  1012	                    .elem("ID", id)
  1013	                    .elem("DisplayName", displayName)
  1014	                  .end("Owner")
  1015	                  .start("AccessControlList")
  1016	                    .start("Grant")
  1017	                      .raw("<Grantee xmlns:xsi=\"http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance\" xsi:type=\"CanonicalUser\">")
  1018	                        .elem("ID", id)
  1019	                        .elem("DisplayName", displayName)
  1020	                      .raw("</Grantee>")
  1021	                      .elem("Permission", "FULL_CONTROL")
  1022	                    .end("Grant")
  1023	                  .end("AccessControlList")
  1024	                .end("AccessControlPolicy")
  1025	                .build();
  1026	    }
  1027	
  1028	    private void fireNotifications(String bucketName, String key, String eventName, S3Object obj) {
  1029	        if (sqsService == null && snsService == null) {
  1030	            return;
  1031	        }
  1032	        Bucket bucket = bucketStore.get(bucketName).orElse(null);
  1033	        if (bucket == null) {
  1034	            return;
  1035	        }
  1036	        NotificationConfiguration config = bucket.getNotificationConfiguration();
  1037	        if (config == null || config.isEmpty()) {
  1038	            return;
  1039	        }
  1040	
  1041	        String region = regionResolver != null ? regionResolver.getDefaultRegion() : "us-east-1";
  1042	        String eventJson = buildS3EventJson(bucketName, key, eventName, obj, region, bucket.isVersioningEnabled());
  1043	
  1044	        for (QueueNotification qn : config.getQueueConfigurations()) {
  1045	            if (qn.events().stream().anyMatch(p -> matchesEvent(p, eventName))) {
  1046	                try {
  1047	                    sqsService.sendMessage(sqsUrlFromArn(qn.queueArn()), eventJson, 0);
  1048	                    LOG.debugv("Fired S3 event {0} to SQS {1}", eventName, qn.queueArn());
  1049	                } catch (Exception e) {
  1050	                    LOG.warnv("Failed to deliver S3 event to SQS {0}: {1}", qn.queueArn(), e.getMessage());
  1051	                }
  1052	            }
  1053	        }
  1054	
  1055	        for (TopicNotification tn : config.getTopicConfigurations()) {
  1056	            if (tn.events().stream().anyMatch(p -> matchesEvent(p, eventName))) {
  1057	                try {
  1058	                    snsService.publish(tn.topicArn(), null, eventJson, "Amazon S3 Notification", region);
  1059	                    LOG.debugv("Fired S3 event {0} to SNS {1}", eventName, tn.topicArn());
  1060	                } catch (Exception e) {
  1061	                    LOG.warnv("Failed to deliver S3 event to SNS {0}: {1}", tn.topicArn(), e.getMessage());
  1062	                }
  1063	            }
  1064	        }
  1065	    }
  1066	
  1067	    private boolean matchesEvent(String pattern, String eventName) {
  1068	        String full = "s3:" + eventName;
  1069	        if (pattern.endsWith("*")) {
  1070	            return full.startsWith(pattern.substring(0, pattern.length() - 1));
  1071	        }
  1072	        return full.equals(pattern);
  1073	    }
  1074	
  1075	    private String sqsUrlFromArn(String arn) {
  1076	        if (arn.split(":").length < 6) return arn;
  1077	        return AwsArnUtils.arnToQueueUrl(arn, baseUrl);
  1078	    }
  1079	
  1080	    private String buildS3EventJson(String bucketName, String key, String eventName,
  1081	                                    S3Object obj, String region, boolean isVersionEnabled) {
  1082	        try {
  1083	            String eventTime = DateTimeFormatter.ISO_INSTANT.format(Instant.now());
  1084	            long size = obj != null ? obj.getSize() : 0;
  1085	            String eTag = obj != null && obj.getETag() != null ? obj.getETag().replace("\"", "") : "";
  1086	            String requestId = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
  1087	
  1088	            ObjectNode bucketNode = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
  1089	            bucketNode.put("name", bucketName);
  1090	            bucketNode.put("arn", "arn:aws:s3:::" + bucketName);
  1091	
  1092	            ObjectNode objectNode = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
  1093	            objectNode.put("key", key);
  1094	            objectNode.put("size", size);
  1095	            objectNode.put("eTag", eTag);
  1096	            if(isVersionEnabled) {
  1097	                String versionId = obj !=null && obj.getVersionId()!=null ? obj.getVersionId() : "";
  1098	                objectNode.put("versionId", versionId);
  1099	            }
  1100	            ObjectNode s3Node = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
  1101	            s3Node.put("s3SchemaVersion", "1.0");
  1102	            s3Node.put("configurationId", "emulator");
  1103	            s3Node.set("bucket", bucketNode);
  1104	            s3Node.set("object", objectNode);
  1105	
  1106	            ObjectNode record = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
  1107	            record.put("eventVersion", "2.1");
  1108	            record.put("eventSource", "aws:s3");
  1109	            record.put("awsRegion", region);
  1110	            record.put("eventTime", eventTime);
  1111	            record.put("eventName", eventName);
  1112	            record.putObject("userIdentity").put("principalId", "AWS:EMULATOR");
  1113	            record.putObject("requestParameters").put("sourceIPAddress", "127.0.0.1");
  1114	            record.putObject("responseElements").put("x-amz-request-id", requestId);
  1115	            record.set("s3", s3Node);
  1116	
  1117	            ObjectNode root = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
  1118	            root.putArray("Records").add(record);
  1119	            return objectMapper.writeValueAsString(root);
  1120	        } catch (Exception e) {
  1121	            return "{\"Records\":[]}";
  1122	        }
  1123	    }
  1124	
  1125	    private void cleanupMultipart(String uploadId) {
  1126	        multipartUploads.remove(uploadId);
  1127	        if (inMemory) {
  1128	            memoryMultipartStore.remove(uploadId);
  1129	        } else {
  1130	            deleteDirectory(dataRoot.resolve(".multipart").resolve(uploadId));
  1131	        }
  1132	    }
  1133	
  1134	    private static S3Checksum buildChecksum(byte[] data, List<Part> parts, boolean multipartUpload) {
  1135	        S3Checksum checksum = new S3Checksum();
  1136	        checksum.setChecksumSHA1(S3Checksum.sha1Base64(data));
  1137	        checksum.setChecksumSHA256(S3Checksum.sha256Base64(data));
  1138	        checksum.setChecksumType(multipartUpload || (parts != null && parts.size() > 1)
  1139	                ? "COMPOSITE"
  1140	                : "FULL_OBJECT");
  1141	        return checksum;
  1142	    }
  1143	
  1144	    private static S3Object copyObject(S3Object source) {
  1145	        S3Object copy = new S3Object();
  1146	        copy.setBucketName(source.getBucketName());
  1147	        copy.setKey(source.getKey());
  1148	        copy.setData(source.getData() != null ? Arrays.copyOf(source.getData(), source.getData().length) : null);
  1149	        copy.setMetadata(new HashMap<>(source.getMetadata()));
  1150	        copy.setContentType(source.getContentType());
  1151	        copy.setSize(source.getSize());
  1152	        copy.setLastModified(source.getLastModified());
  1153	        copy.setETag(source.getETag());
  1154	        copy.setStorageClass(source.getStorageClass());
  1155	        copy.setChecksum(copyChecksum(source.getChecksum()));
  1156	        copy.setParts(copyParts(source.getParts()));
  1157	        copy.setVersionId(source.getVersionId());
  1158	        copy.setDeleteMarker(source.isDeleteMarker());
  1159	        copy.setLatest(source.isLatest());
  1160	        copy.setTags(new HashMap<>(source.getTags()));
  1161	        copy.setObjectLockMode(source.getObjectLockMode());
  1162	        copy.setRetainUntilDate(source.getRetainUntilDate());
  1163	        copy.setLegalHoldStatus(source.getLegalHoldStatus());
  1164	        copy.setAcl(source.getAcl());
  1165	        return copy;
  1166	    }
  1167	
  1168	    private static S3Checksum copyChecksum(S3Checksum source) {
  1169	        if (source == null) {
  1170	            return null;
  1171	        }
  1172	        S3Checksum copy = new S3Checksum();
  1173	        copy.setChecksumCRC32(source.getChecksumCRC32());
  1174	        copy.setChecksumCRC32C(source.getChecksumCRC32C());
  1175	        copy.setChecksumCRC64NVME(source.getChecksumCRC64NVME());
  1176	        copy.setChecksumSHA1(source.getChecksumSHA1());
  1177	        copy.setChecksumSHA256(source.getChecksumSHA256());
  1178	        copy.setChecksumType(source.getChecksumType());
  1179	        return copy;
  1180	    }
  1181	
  1182	    private static List<Part> copyParts(List<Part> sourceParts) {
  1183	        if (sourceParts == null) {
  1184	            return new ArrayList<>();
  1185	        }
  1186	        return sourceParts.stream().map(S3Service::copyPart).toList();
  1187	    }
  1188	
  1189	    private static Part copyPart(Part source) {
  1190	        if (source == null) {
  1191	            return null;
  1192	        }
  1193	        Part copy = new Part();
  1194	        copy.setPartNumber(source.getPartNumber());
  1195	        copy.setETag(source.getETag());
  1196	        copy.setSize(source.getSize());
  1197	        copy.setChecksum(copyChecksum(source.getChecksum()));
  1198	        copy.setLastModified(source.getLastModified());
  1199	        return copy;
  1200	    }
  1201	
  1202	    private static String computeETag(byte[] data) {
  1203	        return "\"" + bytesToHex(computeETagBytes(data)) + "\"";
  1204	    }
  1205	
  1206	    private static byte[] computeETagBytes(byte[] data) {
  1207	        try {
  1208	            return MessageDigest.getInstance("MD5").digest(data);
  1209	        } catch (NoSuchAlgorithmException e) {
  1210	            throw new RuntimeException("MD5 algorithm not available", e);
  1211	        }
  1212	    }
  1213	
  1214	    private static String bytesToHex(byte[] bytes) {
  1215	        var sb = new StringBuilder();
  1216	        for (byte b : bytes) {
  1217	            sb.append(String.format("%02x", b));
  1218	        }
  1219	        return sb.toString();
  1220	    }

  1225	                    "The specified bucket does not exist.", 404);
  1226	        }
  1227	    }

  1229	    private String objectKey(String bucketName, String key) {

  1231	    }

  1233	    private String versionedKey(String bucketName, String key, String versionId) {
  1234	        return bucketName + "/" + key + "#v#" + versionId;
  1235	    }
  1236	
  1237	    private Path resolveObjectPath(String bucketName, String key) {
  1238	        return dataRoot.resolve(bucketName).resolve(key);
  1239	    }
  1240	
  1241	    private Path resolveVersionedPath(String bucketName, String key, String versionId) {
  1242	        return dataRoot.resolve(".versions").resolve(bucketName).resolve(key).resolve(versionId);
  1243	    }
  1244	
  1245	    private void writeVersionedFile(String bucketName, String key, String versionId, byte[] data) {
  1246	        if (inMemory) {
  1247	            memoryDataStore.put(versionedKey(bucketName, key, versionId), data);
  1248	            return;
  1249	        }
  1250	        try {
  1251	            Path filePath = resolveVersionedPath(bucketName, key, versionId);
  1252	            Files.createDirectories(filePath.getParent());
  1253	            Files.write(filePath, data);
  1254	        } catch (IOException e) {
  1255	            throw new UncheckedIOException("Failed to write versioned S3 object file", e);
  1256	        }
  1257	    }
  1258	
  1259	    private byte[] readVersionedFile(String bucketName, String key, String versionId) {
  1260	        if (inMemory) {
  1261	            return memoryDataStore.get(versionedKey(bucketName, key, versionId));
  1262	        }
  1263	        try {
  1264	            return Files.readAllBytes(resolveVersionedPath(bucketName, key, versionId));
  1265	        } catch (IOException e) {
  1266	            throw new UncheckedIOException("Failed to read versioned S3 object file", e);
  1267	        }
  1268	    }
  1269	
  1270	    private void writeFile(String bucketName, String key, byte[] data) {
  1271	        if (inMemory) {
  1272	            memoryDataStore.put(objectKey(bucketName, key), data);
  1273	            return;
  1274	        }
  1275	        try {
  1276	            Path filePath = resolveObjectPath(bucketName, key);
  1277	            Files.createDirectories(filePath.getParent());
  1278	            Files.write(filePath, data);
  1279	        } catch (IOException e) {
  1280	            throw new UncheckedIOException("Failed to write S3 object file", e);
  1281	        }
  1282	    }
  1283	
  1284	    private byte[] readFile(String bucketName, String key) {
  1285	        if (inMemory) {
  1286	            return memoryDataStore.get(objectKey(bucketName, key));
  1287	        }
  1288	        try {
  1289	            return Files.readAllBytes(resolveObjectPath(bucketName, key));
  1290	        } catch (IOException e) {
  1291	            throw new UncheckedIOException("Failed to read S3 object file", e);
  1292	        }
  1293	    }
  1294	
  1295	    private void deleteFile(String bucketName, String key) {
  1296	        if (inMemory) {
  1297	            memoryDataStore.remove(objectKey(bucketName, key));
  1298	            return;
  1299	        }
  1300	        try {
  1301	            Files.deleteIfExists(resolveObjectPath(bucketName, key));
  1302	        } catch (IOException e) {
  1303	            LOG.errorv(e, "Failed to delete S3 object file: {0}/{1}", bucketName, key);
  1304	        }
  1305	    }
  1306	
  1307	    private void deleteDirectory(Path dir) {
  1308	        if (!Files.exists(dir)) return;
  1309	        try (var walk = Files.walk(dir)) {
  1310	            walk.sorted(Comparator.reverseOrder()).forEach(path -> {
  1311	                try {
  1312	                    Files.deleteIfExists(path);
  1313	                } catch (IOException e) {
  1314	                    LOG.errorv(e, "Failed to delete: {0}", path);
  1315	                }
  1316	            });
  1317	        } catch (IOException e) {
  1318	            LOG.errorv(e, "Failed to delete directory: {0}", dir);
  1319	        }
  1320	    }
  1321	}
