    40	/**
    41	 * S3 controller handling REST-style S3 API requests.
    42	 * Routes: /{bucket} for bucket ops, /{bucket}/{key+} for object ops.
    43	 */
    44	@Path("/")
    45	public class S3Controller {
    46	
    47	    private static final Logger LOG = Logger.getLogger(S3Controller.class);
    48	    private static final DateTimeFormatter ISO_FORMAT = DateTimeFormatter.ISO_INSTANT;
    49	    private static final DateTimeFormatter RFC_822 = DateTimeFormatter
    50	            .ofPattern("EEE, dd MMM yyyy HH:mm:ss z", Locale.US)
    51	            .withZone(ZoneId.of("GMT"));
    52	
    53	    private final S3Service s3Service;
    54	    private final S3SelectService s3SelectService;
    55	    private final RegionResolver regionResolver;
    56	
    57	    @Inject
    58	    public S3Controller(S3Service s3Service, S3SelectService s3SelectService,
    59	                        RegionResolver regionResolver) {
    60	        this.s3Service = s3Service;
    61	        this.s3SelectService = s3SelectService;
    62	        this.regionResolver = regionResolver;
    63	    }
    64	
    65	    // --- Bucket operations ---
    66	
    67	    @GET
    68	    @Produces(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML)
    69	    public Response listBuckets(@HeaderParam("X-Amz-Target") String target) {
    70	        if (target != null) {
    71	            return null;
    72	        }
    73	        try {
    74	            List<Bucket> buckets = s3Service.listBuckets();
    75	            XmlBuilder xml = new XmlBuilder()
    76	                    .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
    77	                    .start("ListAllMyBucketsResult", AwsNamespaces.S3)
    78	                    .start("Owner")
    79	                    .elem("ID", "owner")
    80	                    .elem("DisplayName", "owner")
    81	                    .end("Owner")
    82	                    .start("Buckets");
    83	            for (Bucket b : buckets) {
    84	                xml.start("Bucket")
    85	                   .elem("Name", b.getName())
    86	                   .elem("CreationDate", ISO_FORMAT.format(b.getCreationDate()))
    87	                   .end("Bucket");
    88	            }
    89	            xml.end("Buckets").end("ListAllMyBucketsResult");
    90	            return Response.ok(xml.build()).build();
    91	        } catch (AwsException e) {
    92	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
    93	        }
    94	    }
    95	
    96	    @HEAD
    97	    @Path("/{bucket}")
    98	    public Response headBucket(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket) {
    99	        try {
   100	            s3Service.headBucket(bucket);
   101	            String bucketRegion = s3Service.getBucketRegion(bucket);
   102	            if (bucketRegion == null || bucketRegion.isBlank()) {
   103	                bucketRegion = regionResolver.getDefaultRegion();
   104	            }
   105	            return Response.ok()
   106	                    .header("x-amz-bucket-region", bucketRegion)
   107	                    .build();
   108	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   109	            return Response.status(e.getHttpStatus()).build();
   110	        }
   111	    }
   112	
   113	    @PUT
   114	    @Path("/{bucket}")
   115	    public Response createBucket(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket,
   116	                                  @Context UriInfo uriInfo,
   117	                                  @Context HttpHeaders httpHeaders,
   118	                                  byte[] body) {
   119	        try {
   120	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "notification")) {
   121	                return handlePutBucketNotification(bucket, body);
   122	            }
   123	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "versioning")) {
   124	                return handlePutBucketVersioning(bucket, body);
   125	            }
   126	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "tagging")) {
   127	                return handlePutBucketTagging(bucket, body);
   128	            }
   129	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "object-lock")) {
   130	                return handlePutObjectLockConfiguration(bucket, body);
   131	            }
   132	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "policy")) {
   133	                s3Service.putBucketPolicy(bucket, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   134	                return Response.ok().build();
   135	            }
   136	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "cors")) {
   137	                s3Service.putBucketCors(bucket, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   138	                return Response.ok().build();
   139	            }
   140	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "lifecycle")) {
   141	                s3Service.putBucketLifecycle(bucket, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   142	                return Response.ok().build();
   143	            }
   144	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "acl")) {
   145	                s3Service.putBucketAcl(bucket, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   146	                return Response.ok().build();
   147	            }
   148	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "encryption")) {
   149	                s3Service.putBucketEncryption(bucket, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   150	                return Response.ok().build();
   151	            }
   152	
   153	            String locationConstraint = null;
   154	            if (body != null && body.length > 0) {
   155	                locationConstraint = XmlParser.extractFirst(new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8),
   156	                        "LocationConstraint", null);
   157	            }
   158	            if (locationConstraint != null) {
   159	                locationConstraint = locationConstraint.trim();
   160	                if (locationConstraint.isEmpty()) {
   161	                    locationConstraint = null;
   162	                } else if ("us-east-1".equalsIgnoreCase(locationConstraint)) {
   163	                    throw new AwsException("InvalidLocationConstraint",
   164	                            "The specified location-constraint is not valid.", 400);
   165	                }
   166	            }
   167	            String region = locationConstraint != null ? locationConstraint : regionResolver.resolveRegion(httpHeaders);
   168	            s3Service.createBucket(bucket, region);
   169	            String lockEnabled = httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-bucket-object-lock-enabled");
   170	            if ("true".equalsIgnoreCase(lockEnabled)) {
   171	                s3Service.putBucketVersioning(bucket, "Enabled");
   172	                s3Service.setBucketObjectLockEnabled(bucket);
   173	            }
   174	            return Response.ok()
   175	                    .header("Location", "/" + bucket)
   176	                    .build();
   177	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   178	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
   179	        }
   180	    }
   181	
   182	    @DELETE
   183	    @Path("/{bucket}")
   184	    public Response deleteBucket(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket,
   185	                                  @Context UriInfo uriInfo) {
   186	        try {
   187	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "tagging")) {
   188	                s3Service.deleteBucketTagging(bucket);
   189	                return Response.noContent().build();
   190	            }
   191	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "policy")) {
   192	                s3Service.deleteBucketPolicy(bucket);
   193	                return Response.noContent().build();
   194	            }
   195	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "cors")) {
   196	                s3Service.deleteBucketCors(bucket);
   197	                return Response.noContent().build();
   198	            }
   199	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "lifecycle")) {
   200	                s3Service.deleteBucketLifecycle(bucket);
   201	                return Response.noContent().build();
   202	            }
   203	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "encryption")) {
   204	                s3Service.deleteBucketEncryption(bucket);
   205	                return Response.noContent().build();
   206	            }
   207	            s3Service.deleteBucket(bucket);
   208	            return Response.noContent().build();
   209	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   210	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
   211	        }
   212	    }
   213	
   214	    @GET
   215	    @Path("/{bucket}")
   216	    @Produces(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML)
   217	    public Response listObjects(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket,
   218	                                @QueryParam("prefix") String prefix,
   219	                                @QueryParam("delimiter") String delimiter,
   220	                                @QueryParam("max-keys") Integer maxKeys,
   221	                                @QueryParam("list-type") String listType,
   222	                                @QueryParam("continuation-token") String continuationToken,
   223	                                @QueryParam("start-after") String startAfter,
   224	                                @Context UriInfo uriInfo) {
   225	        try {
   226	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "uploads")) {
   227	                return handleListMultipartUploads(bucket);
   228	            }
   229	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "notification")) {
   230	                return handleGetBucketNotification(bucket);
   231	            }
   232	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "versioning")) {
   233	                return handleGetBucketVersioning(bucket);
   234	            }
   235	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "versions")) {
   236	                return handleListObjectVersions(bucket, prefix, maxKeys);
   237	            }
   238	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "location")) {
   239	                return handleGetBucketLocation(bucket);
   240	            }
   241	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "tagging")) {
   242	                return handleGetBucketTagging(bucket);
   243	            }
   244	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "object-lock")) {
   245	                return handleGetObjectLockConfiguration(bucket);
   246	            }
   247	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "policy")) {
   248	                return Response.ok(s3Service.getBucketPolicy(bucket)).build();
   249	            }
   250	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "cors")) {
   251	                return Response.ok(s3Service.getBucketCors(bucket)).build();
   252	            }
   253	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "lifecycle")) {
   254	                return Response.ok(s3Service.getBucketLifecycle(bucket)).build();
   255	            }
   256	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "acl")) {
   257	                return Response.ok(s3Service.getBucketAcl(bucket)).build();
   258	            }
   259	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "encryption")) {
   260	                return Response.ok(s3Service.getBucketEncryption(bucket)).build();
   261	            }
   262	
   263	            int max = (maxKeys != null && maxKeys > 0) ? maxKeys : 1000;
   264	            List<S3Object> objects = s3Service.listObjects(bucket, prefix, delimiter, max);
   265	            boolean v2 = "2".equals(listType);
   266	
   267	            XmlBuilder xml = new XmlBuilder()
   268	                    .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
   269	                    .start("ListBucketResult", AwsNamespaces.S3)
   270	                    .elem("Name", bucket)
   271	                    .elem("Prefix", prefix)
   272	                    .elem("Delimiter", delimiter)
   273	                    .elem("MaxKeys", max);
   274	            if (v2) {
   275	                xml.elem("KeyCount", objects.size());
   276	            }
   277	            xml.elem("IsTruncated", false);
   278	            for (S3Object obj : objects) {
   279	                xml.start("Contents")
   280	                   .elem("Key", obj.getKey())
   281	                   .elem("LastModified", ISO_FORMAT.format(obj.getLastModified()))
   282	                   .elem("ETag", obj.getETag())
   283	                   .elem("Size", obj.getSize())
   284	                   .elem("StorageClass", obj.getStorageClass())
   285	                   .end("Contents");
   286	            }
   287	            xml.end("ListBucketResult");
   288	            return Response.ok(xml.build()).build();
   289	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   290	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
   291	        }
   292	    }
   293	
   294	    // --- Object operations ---
   295	
   296	    @PUT
   297	    @Path("/{bucket}/{key:.+}")
   298	    public Response putObject(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket,
   299	                              @PathParam("key") String key,
   300	                              @HeaderParam("Content-Type") String contentType,
   301	                              @HeaderParam("Content-Encoding") String contentEncoding,
   302	                              @HeaderParam("x-amz-content-sha256") String contentSha256,
   303	                              @HeaderParam("x-amz-copy-source") String copySource,
   304	                              @QueryParam("uploadId") String uploadId,
   305	                              @QueryParam("partNumber") Integer partNumber,
   306	                              @Context UriInfo uriInfo,
   307	                              @Context HttpHeaders httpHeaders,
   308	                              byte[] body) {
   309	        try {
   310	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "tagging")) {
   311	                return handlePutObjectTagging(bucket, key, body);
   312	            }
   313	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "retention")) {
   314	                return handlePutObjectRetention(bucket, key,
   315	                        uriInfo.getQueryParameters().getFirst("versionId"), httpHeaders, body);
   316	            }
   317	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "legal-hold")) {
   318	                return handlePutObjectLegalHold(bucket, key,
   319	                        uriInfo.getQueryParameters().getFirst("versionId"), body);
   320	            }
   321	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "acl")) {
   322	                s3Service.putObjectAcl(bucket, key, uriInfo.getQueryParameters().getFirst("versionId"),
   323	                        new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   324	                return Response.ok().build();
   325	            }
   326	
   327	            if (uploadId != null && partNumber != null) {
   328	                byte[] partData = decodeAwsChunked(body, contentEncoding, contentSha256);
   329	                validateChecksumHeaders(httpHeaders, partData);
   330	                String eTag = s3Service.uploadPart(bucket, key, uploadId, partNumber, partData);
   331	                return Response.ok().header("ETag", eTag).build();
   332	            }
   333	
   334	            if (copySource != null && !copySource.isEmpty()) {
   335	                return handleCopyObject(copySource, bucket, key, contentType, httpHeaders);
   336	            }
   337	
   338	            String lockMode = httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-object-lock-mode");
   339	            String retainUntilStr = httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-object-lock-retain-until-date");
   340	            String legalHold = httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-object-lock-legal-hold");
   341	            Instant retainUntil = retainUntilStr != null ? Instant.parse(retainUntilStr) : null;
   342	
   343	            byte[] data = decodeAwsChunked(body, contentEncoding, contentSha256);
   344	            validateChecksumHeaders(httpHeaders, data);
   345	            S3Object obj = s3Service.putObject(bucket, key, data, contentType, extractUserMetadata(httpHeaders),
   346	                    httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-storage-class"),
   347	                    lockMode, retainUntil, legalHold);
   348	            var resp = Response.ok().header("ETag", obj.getETag());
   349	            if (obj.getVersionId() != null) {
   350	                resp.header("x-amz-version-id", obj.getVersionId());
   351	            }
   352	            appendObjectHeaders(resp, obj);
   353	            return resp.build();
   354	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   355	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
   356	        }
   357	    }
   358	
   359	    @GET
   360	    @Path("/{bucket}/{key:.+}")
   361	    public Response getObject(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket,
   362	                              @PathParam("key") String key,
   363	                              @QueryParam("versionId") String versionId,
   364	                              @HeaderParam("x-amz-object-attributes") String objectAttributesHeader,
   365	                              @HeaderParam("x-amz-max-parts") Integer maxParts,
   366	                              @HeaderParam("x-amz-part-number-marker") Integer partNumberMarker,
   367	                              @HeaderParam("If-Match") String ifMatch,
   368	                              @HeaderParam("If-None-Match") String ifNoneMatch,
   369	                              @HeaderParam("If-Modified-Since") String ifModifiedSince,
   370	                              @HeaderParam("If-Unmodified-Since") String ifUnmodifiedSince,
   371	                              @HeaderParam("Range") String rangeHeader,
   372	                              @Context UriInfo uriInfo,
   373	                              @Context HttpHeaders httpHeaders) {
   374	        try {
   375	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "tagging")) {
   376	                return handleGetObjectTagging(bucket, key);
   377	            }
   378	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "retention")) {
   379	                return handleGetObjectRetention(bucket, key, versionId);
   380	            }
   381	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "legal-hold")) {
   382	                return handleGetObjectLegalHold(bucket, key, versionId);
   383	            }
   384	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "acl")) {
   385	                return Response.ok(s3Service.getObjectAcl(bucket, key, versionId)).build();
   386	            }
   387	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "attributes")) {
   388	                // Merge all x-amz-object-attributes header values (SDK may send multiple lines)
   389	                List<String> attrHeaders = httpHeaders.getRequestHeader("x-amz-object-attributes");
   390	                String mergedAttributes = attrHeaders != null ? String.join(",", attrHeaders) : objectAttributesHeader;
   391	                return handleGetObjectAttributes(bucket, key, versionId,
   392	                        mergedAttributes, maxParts, partNumberMarker);
   393	            }
   394	            if (hasPreconditions(ifMatch, ifNoneMatch, ifModifiedSince, ifUnmodifiedSince)) {
   395	                // Fetch metadata only to evaluate preconditions, avoiding loading the full object unnecessarily.
   396	                S3Object metadata = s3Service.headObject(bucket, key, versionId);
   397	                Response preconditionResponse = checkPreconditions(metadata, ifMatch, ifNoneMatch, ifModifiedSince, ifUnmodifiedSince);
   398	                if (preconditionResponse != null) {
   399	                    return preconditionResponse;
   400	                }
   401	            }
   402	            S3Object obj = s3Service.getObject(bucket, key, versionId);
   403	
   404	            if (rangeHeader != null && rangeHeader.startsWith("bytes=")) {
   405	                return handleRangeRequest(obj, rangeHeader);
   406	            }
   407	
   408	            var resp = Response.ok(obj.getData())
   409	                    .header("Content-Type", obj.getContentType())
   410	                    .header("Content-Length", obj.getSize())
   411	                    .header("ETag", obj.getETag())
   412	                    .header("Last-Modified", RFC_822.format(obj.getLastModified()))
   413	                    .header("Accept-Ranges", "bytes");
   414	            if (obj.getVersionId() != null) {
   415	                resp.header("x-amz-version-id", obj.getVersionId());
   416	            }
   417	            appendObjectHeaders(resp, obj);
   418	            return resp.build();
   419	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   420	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
   421	        }
   422	    }
   423	
   424	    private Response handleRangeRequest(S3Object obj, String rangeHeader) {
   425	        byte[] data = obj.getData();
   426	        int totalSize = data.length;
   427	        String rangeSpec = rangeHeader.substring("bytes=".length()).trim();
   428	
   429	        int start, end;
   430	        try {
   431	            int dash = rangeSpec.indexOf('-');
   432	            if (dash < 0) {
   433	                return invalidRangeResponse(totalSize);
   434	            }
   435	            String before = rangeSpec.substring(0, dash);
   436	            String after = rangeSpec.substring(dash + 1);
   437	            if (before.isEmpty() && after.isEmpty()) {
   438	                return invalidRangeResponse(totalSize);
   439	            }
   440	            if (before.isEmpty()) {
   441	                int suffix = Integer.parseInt(after);
   442	                if (suffix <= 0) {
   443	                    return invalidRangeResponse(totalSize);
   444	                }
   445	                start = Math.max(0, totalSize - suffix);
   446	                end = totalSize - 1;
   447	            } else {
   448	                start = Integer.parseInt(before);
   449	                end = after.isEmpty() ? totalSize - 1 : Math.min(Integer.parseInt(after), totalSize - 1);
   450	            }
   451	        } catch (NumberFormatException e) {
   452	            return invalidRangeResponse(totalSize);
   453	        }
   454	
   455	        if (start < 0 || start >= totalSize || start > end) {
   456	            return invalidRangeResponse(totalSize);
   457	        }
   458	
   459	        byte[] rangeData = java.util.Arrays.copyOfRange(data, start, end + 1);
   460	        return Response.status(206)
   461	                .entity(rangeData)
   462	                .header("Content-Type", obj.getContentType())
   463	                .header("Content-Length", rangeData.length)
   464	                .header("Content-Range", "bytes " + start + "-" + end + "/" + totalSize)
   465	                .header("ETag", obj.getETag())
   466	                .header("Last-Modified", RFC_822.format(obj.getLastModified()))
   467	                .header("Accept-Ranges", "bytes")
   468	                .build();
   469	    }
   470	
   471	    private Response invalidRangeResponse(int totalSize) {
   472	        String xml = new XmlBuilder()
   473	                .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
   474	                .start("Error")
   475	                .elem("Code", "InvalidRange")
   476	                .elem("Message", "The requested range is not satisfiable.")
   477	                .elem("RequestId", java.util.UUID.randomUUID().toString())
   478	                .end("Error")
   479	                .build();
   480	        return Response.status(416)
   481	                .entity(xml)
   482	                .type(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML)
   483	                .header("Content-Range", "bytes */" + totalSize)
   484	                .build();
   485	    }
   486	
   487	    @HEAD
   488	    @Path("/{bucket}/{key:.+}")
   489	    public Response headObject(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket,
   490	                               @PathParam("key") String key,
   491	                               @QueryParam("versionId") String versionId,
   492	                               @HeaderParam("If-Match") String ifMatch,
   493	                               @HeaderParam("If-None-Match") String ifNoneMatch,
   494	                               @HeaderParam("If-Modified-Since") String ifModifiedSince,
   495	                               @HeaderParam("If-Unmodified-Since") String ifUnmodifiedSince) {
   496	        try {
   497	            S3Object obj = s3Service.headObject(bucket, key, versionId);
   498	            Response preconditionResponse = checkPreconditions(obj, ifMatch, ifNoneMatch, ifModifiedSince, ifUnmodifiedSince);
   499	            if (preconditionResponse != null) {
   500	                return preconditionResponse;
   501	            }
   502	            var resp = Response.ok()
   503	                    .header("Content-Type", obj.getContentType())
   504	                    .header("Content-Length", obj.getSize())
   505	                    .header("ETag", obj.getETag())
   506	                    .header("Last-Modified", RFC_822.format(obj.getLastModified()))
   507	                    .header("Accept-Ranges", "bytes");
   508	            if (obj.getVersionId() != null) {
   509	                resp.header("x-amz-version-id", obj.getVersionId());
   510	            }
   511	            appendObjectHeaders(resp, obj);
   512	            return resp.build();
   513	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   514	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
   515	        }
   516	    }
   517	
   518	    @DELETE
   519	    @Path("/{bucket}/{key:.+}")
   520	    public Response deleteObject(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket,
   521	                                 @PathParam("key") String key,
   522	                                 @QueryParam("uploadId") String uploadId,
   523	                                 @QueryParam("versionId") String versionId,
   524	                                 @Context UriInfo uriInfo,
   525	                                 @Context HttpHeaders httpHeaders) {
   526	        try {
   527	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "tagging")) {
   528	                s3Service.deleteObjectTagging(bucket, key);
   529	                return Response.noContent().build();
   530	            }
   531	            if (uploadId != null) {
   532	                s3Service.abortMultipartUpload(bucket, key, uploadId);
   533	                return Response.noContent().build();
   534	            }
   535	            boolean bypass = "true".equalsIgnoreCase(
   536	                    httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-bypass-governance-retention"));
   537	            S3Object result = s3Service.deleteObject(bucket, key, versionId, bypass);
   538	            var resp = Response.noContent();
   539	            if (result != null && result.isDeleteMarker()) {
   540	                resp.header("x-amz-delete-marker", "true");
   541	                resp.header("x-amz-version-id", result.getVersionId());
   542	            }
   543	            return resp.build();
   544	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   545	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
   546	        }
   547	    }
   548	
   549	    // --- Batch Delete (DeleteObjects) ---
   550	
   551	    @POST
   552	    @Path("/{bucket}")
   553	    @Produces(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML)
   554	    public Response handleBucketPost(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket,
   555	                                      @Context UriInfo uriInfo,
   556	                                      byte[] body) {
   557	        try {
   558	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "delete")) {
   559	                return handleDeleteObjects(bucket, body);
   560	            }
   561	            return xmlErrorResponse(new AwsException("InvalidArgument",
   562	                    "POST on bucket requires ?delete parameter.", 400));
   563	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   564	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
   565	        }
   566	    }
   567	
   568	    @POST
   569	    @Path("/{bucket}/{key:.+}")
   570	    @Produces(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML)
   571	    public Response handleMultipartPost(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket,
   572	                                         @PathParam("key") String key,
   573	                                         @QueryParam("uploadId") String uploadId,
   574	                                         @QueryParam("versionId") String versionId,
   575	                                         @HeaderParam("Content-Type") String contentType,
   576	                                         @Context HttpHeaders httpHeaders,
   577	                                         @Context UriInfo uriInfo,
   578	                                         byte[] body) {
   579	        try {
   580	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "uploads")) {
   581	                MultipartUpload upload = s3Service.initiateMultipartUpload(bucket, key, contentType,
   582	                        extractUserMetadata(httpHeaders), httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-storage-class"));
   583	                String xml = new XmlBuilder()
   584	                        .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
   585	                        .start("InitiateMultipartUploadResult", AwsNamespaces.S3)
   586	                        .elem("Bucket", bucket)
   587	                        .elem("Key", key)
   588	                        .elem("UploadId", upload.getUploadId())
   589	                        .end("InitiateMultipartUploadResult")
   590	                        .build();
   591	                return Response.ok(xml).build();
   592	            }
   593	
   594	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "restore")) {
   595	                s3Service.restoreObject(bucket, key, versionId, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   596	                return Response.accepted().build();
   597	            }
   598	
   599	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "select")) {
   600	                S3Object obj = s3Service.getObject(bucket, key, versionId);
   601	                byte[] result = s3SelectService.select(obj, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   602	                return Response.ok(result)
   603	                        .type("application/octet-stream")
   604	                        .build();
   605	            }
   606	
   607	            if (uploadId != null) {
   608	                List<Integer> partNumbers = parseCompleteMultipartBody(new String(body));
   609	                S3Object obj = s3Service.completeMultipartUpload(bucket, key, uploadId, partNumbers);
   610	                String baseUrl = uriInfo.getBaseUri().toString();
   611	                if (baseUrl.endsWith("/")) {
   612	                    baseUrl = baseUrl.substring(0, baseUrl.length() - 1);
   613	                }
   614	                XmlBuilder xmlBuilder = new XmlBuilder()
   615	                        .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
   616	                        .start("CompleteMultipartUploadResult", AwsNamespaces.S3)
   617	                        .elem("Location", baseUrl + "/" + bucket + "/" + key)
   618	                        .elem("Bucket", bucket)
   619	                        .elem("Key", key)
   620	                        .elem("ETag", obj.getETag());
   621	                if (obj.getVersionId() != null) {
   622	                    xmlBuilder.elem("VersionId", obj.getVersionId());
   623	                }
   624	                String xml = xmlBuilder.end("CompleteMultipartUploadResult").build();
   625	                var resp = Response.ok(xml);
   626	                if (obj.getVersionId() != null) {
   627	                    resp.header("x-amz-version-id", obj.getVersionId());
   628	                }
   629	                return resp.build();
   630	            }
   631	
   632	            return xmlErrorResponse(new AwsException("InvalidArgument",
   633	                    "POST requires either ?uploads, ?uploadId, ?restore or ?select parameter.", 400));
   634	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   635	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
   636	        }
   637	    }
   638	
   639	    private Response handleDeleteObjects(String bucket, byte[] body) {
   640	        String xml = new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
   641	        List<String> keys = XmlParser.extractAll(xml, "Key");
   642	        boolean quiet = XmlParser.containsValue(xml, "Quiet", "true");
   643	        S3Service.DeleteObjectsResult result = s3Service.deleteObjects(bucket, keys);
   644	
   645	        XmlBuilder builder = new XmlBuilder()
   646	                .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
   647	                .start("DeleteResult", AwsNamespaces.S3);
   648	        if (!quiet) {
   649	            for (S3Service.DeleteResult d : result.deleted()) {
   650	                builder.start("Deleted").elem("Key", d.key());
   651	                if (d.deleteMarker()) {
   652	                    builder.elem("DeleteMarker", true);
   653	                    if (d.deleteMarkerVersionId() != null) {
   654	                        builder.elem("DeleteMarkerVersionId", d.deleteMarkerVersionId());
   655	                    }
   656	                }
   657	                builder.end("Deleted");
   658	            }
   659	        }
   660	        for (S3Service.DeleteError e : result.errors()) {
   661	            builder.start("Error")
   662	                   .elem("Key", e.key())
   663	                   .elem("Code", e.code())
   664	                   .elem("Message", e.message())
   665	                   .end("Error");
   666	        }
   667	        builder.end("DeleteResult");
   668	        return Response.ok(builder.build()).type(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML).build();
   669	    }
   670	
   671	    private Response handleListMultipartUploads(String bucket) {
   672	        List<MultipartUpload> uploads = s3Service.listMultipartUploads(bucket);
   673	        XmlBuilder xml = new XmlBuilder()
   674	                .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
   675	                .start("ListMultipartUploadsResult", AwsNamespaces.S3)
   676	                .elem("Bucket", bucket);
   677	        for (MultipartUpload upload : uploads) {
   678	            xml.start("Upload")
   679	               .elem("Key", upload.getKey())
   680	               .elem("UploadId", upload.getUploadId())
   681	               .elem("Initiated", ISO_FORMAT.format(upload.getInitiated()))
   682	               .end("Upload");
   683	        }
   684	        xml.end("ListMultipartUploadsResult");
   685	        return Response.ok(xml.build()).build();
   686	    }
   687	
   688	    private List<Integer> parseCompleteMultipartBody(String xml) {
   689	        List<String> parts = XmlParser.extractAll(xml, "PartNumber");
   690	        if (parts.isEmpty()) {
   691	            throw new AwsException("MalformedXML",
   692	                    "The XML you provided was not well-formed.", 400);
   693	        }
   694	        return parts.stream().map(Integer::parseInt).toList();
   695	    }

   714	                .start("VersioningConfiguration", AwsNamespaces.S3);

   716	            xml.elem("Status", status);

   722	    private Response handleListObjectVersions(String bucket, String prefix, Integer maxKeys) {
   723	        int max = (maxKeys != null && maxKeys > 0) ? maxKeys : 1000;
   724	        List<S3Object> versions = s3Service.listObjectVersions(bucket, prefix, max);
   725	        XmlBuilder xml = new XmlBuilder()
   726	                .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
   727	                .start("ListVersionsResult", AwsNamespaces.S3)
   728	                .elem("Name", bucket)
   729	                .elem("Prefix", prefix)
   730	                .elem("MaxKeys", max);
   731	        for (S3Object obj : versions) {
   732	            if (obj.isDeleteMarker()) {
   733	                xml.start("DeleteMarker")
   734	                   .elem("Key", obj.getKey())
   735	                   .elem("VersionId", obj.getVersionId())
   736	                   .elem("IsLatest", obj.isLatest())
   737	                   .elem("LastModified", ISO_FORMAT.format(obj.getLastModified()))
   738	                   .end("DeleteMarker");
   739	            } else {
   740	                xml.start("Version")
   741	                   .elem("Key", obj.getKey())
   742	                   .elem("VersionId", obj.getVersionId())
   743	                   .elem("IsLatest", obj.isLatest())
   744	                   .elem("LastModified", ISO_FORMAT.format(obj.getLastModified()))
   745	                   .elem("ETag", obj.getETag())
   746	                   .elem("Size", obj.getSize())
   747	                   .elem("StorageClass", obj.getStorageClass())
   748	                   .end("Version");
   749	            }
   750	        }
   751	        xml.end("ListVersionsResult");
   752	        return Response.ok(xml.build()).type(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML).build();
   753	    }

   755	    // --- Notification Configuration ---
   756	
   757	    private Response handleGetBucketNotification(String bucket) {
   758	        try {
   759	            NotificationConfiguration config = s3Service.getBucketNotificationConfiguration(bucket);
   760	            XmlBuilder xml = new XmlBuilder()
   761	                    .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
   762	                    .start("NotificationConfiguration", AwsNamespaces.S3);
   763	            for (QueueNotification qn : config.getQueueConfigurations()) {
   764	                xml.start("QueueConfiguration")
   765	                   .elem("Id", qn.id())
   766	                   .elem("Queue", qn.queueArn());
   767	                for (String event : qn.events()) {
   768	                    xml.elem("Event", event);
   769	                }
   770	                xml.end("QueueConfiguration");
   771	            }
   772	            for (TopicNotification tn : config.getTopicConfigurations()) {
   773	                xml.start("TopicConfiguration")
   774	                   .elem("Id", tn.id())
   775	                   .elem("Topic", tn.topicArn());
   776	                for (String event : tn.events()) {
   777	                    xml.elem("Event", event);
   778	                }
   779	                xml.end("TopicConfiguration");
   780	            }
   781	            xml.end("NotificationConfiguration");
   782	            return Response.ok(xml.build()).type(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML).build();
   783	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   784	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
   785	        }
   786	    }
   787	
   788	    private Response handlePutBucketNotification(String bucket, byte[] body) {
   789	        try {
   790	            String xml = new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
   791	            NotificationConfiguration config = new NotificationConfiguration();
   792	
   793	            var queueConfigs = XmlParser.extractGroupsMulti(xml, "QueueConfiguration");
   794	            for (var group : queueConfigs) {
   795	                String id = group.getOrDefault("Id", List.of("")).get(0);
   796	                List<String> queueArns = group.get("Queue");
   797	                List<String> events = group.get("Event");
   798	                if (queueArns != null && !queueArns.isEmpty() && events != null && !events.isEmpty()) {
   799	                    config.getQueueConfigurations().add(new QueueNotification(id, queueArns.get(0), events));
   800	                }
   801	            }
   802	
   803	            var topicConfigs = XmlParser.extractGroupsMulti(xml, "TopicConfiguration");
   804	            for (var group : topicConfigs) {
   805	                String id = group.getOrDefault("Id", List.of("")).get(0);
   806	                List<String> topicArns = group.get("Topic");
   807	                List<String> events = group.get("Event");
   808	                if (topicArns != null && !topicArns.isEmpty() && events != null && !events.isEmpty()) {
   809	                    config.getTopicConfigurations().add(new TopicNotification(id, topicArns.get(0), events));
   810	                }
   811	            }
   812	
   813	            s3Service.putBucketNotificationConfiguration(bucket, config);
   814	            return Response.ok().build();
   815	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   816	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
   817	        }
   818	    }
   819	
   820	    // --- AWS Chunked Decoding ---
   821	
   822	    /**
   823	     * Decodes aws-chunked transfer encoding used by AWS SDK v2 with SigV4 chunk signing.
   824	     * Format: hex-size;chunk-signature=sig\r\n data \r\n ... 0;chunk-signature=sig\r\n
   825	     */
   826	    private byte[] decodeAwsChunked(byte[] body, String contentEncoding, String contentSha256) {
   827	        boolean isAwsChunked = (contentEncoding != null && contentEncoding.contains("aws-chunked"))
   828	                || "STREAMING-AWS4-HMAC-SHA256-PAYLOAD".equals(contentSha256)
   829	                || "STREAMING-AWS4-HMAC-SHA256-PAYLOAD-TRAILER".equals(contentSha256);
   830	        if (!isAwsChunked) {
   831	            return body;
   832	        }
   833	
   834	        try {
   835	            ByteArrayOutputStream out = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
   836	            String raw = new String(body, StandardCharsets.ISO_8859_1);
   837	            int pos = 0;
   838	            while (pos < raw.length()) {
   839	                int lineEnd = raw.indexOf('\n', pos);
   840	                if (lineEnd < 0) break;
   841	                String line = raw.substring(pos, lineEnd).trim();
   842	                int semiColon = line.indexOf(';');
   843	                String hexSize = semiColon >= 0 ? line.substring(0, semiColon) : line;
   844	                int chunkSize = Integer.parseInt(hexSize.trim(), 16);
   845	                if (chunkSize == 0) break;
   846	
   847	                int dataStart = lineEnd + 1;
   848	                byte[] chunkData = new byte[chunkSize];
   849	                System.arraycopy(body, dataStart, chunkData, 0, chunkSize);
   850	                out.write(chunkData);
   851	
   852	                pos = dataStart + chunkSize;
   853	                if (pos < raw.length() && raw.charAt(pos) == '\r') pos++;
   854	                if (pos < raw.length() && raw.charAt(pos) == '\n') pos++;
   855	            }
   856	            return out.toByteArray();
   857	        } catch (Exception e) {
   858	            LOG.debugv("Failed to decode aws-chunked body, using raw: {0}", e.getMessage());
   859	            return body;
   860	        }
   861	    }
   862

   864	
   865	    private Response handleGetBucketLocation(String bucket) {
   866	        String region = s3Service.getBucketRegion(bucket);
   867	        if (region == null) {
   868	            region = regionResolver.getDefaultRegion();
   869	        }
   870	        String xml = new XmlBuilder()
   871	                .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
   872	                .start("LocationConstraint", AwsNamespaces.S3)
   873	                .raw(XmlBuilder.escape(region))
   874	                .end("LocationConstraint")
   875	                .build();
   876	        return Response.ok(xml).type(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML).build();
   877	    }

   895	    private Response handlePutObjectTagging(String bucket, String key, byte[] body) {
   896	        String xml = new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
   897	        Map<String, String> tags = XmlParser.extractPairs(xml, "Tag", "Key", "Value");
   898	        s3Service.putObjectTagging(bucket, key, tags);
   899	        return Response.ok().build();
   900	    }

   902	    private Response handleGetObjectTagging(String bucket, String key) {
   903	        Map<String, String> tags = s3Service.getObjectTagging(bucket, key);
   904	        return Response.ok(buildTaggingXml(tags)).type(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML).build();
   905	    }
   906	
   907	    private String buildTaggingXml(Map<String, String> tags) {
   908	        XmlBuilder xml = new XmlBuilder()
   909	                .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
   910	                .start("Tagging", AwsNamespaces.S3)
   911	                .start("TagSet");
   912	        for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : tags.entrySet()) {
   913	            xml.start("Tag")
   914	               .elem("Key", entry.getKey())
   915	               .elem("Value", entry.getValue())
   916	               .end("Tag");
   917	        }
   918	        xml.end("TagSet").end("Tagging");
   919	        return xml.build();
   920	    }
   921	
   922	    // --- Object Lock Configuration ---
   923	
   924	    private Response handlePutObjectLockConfiguration(String bucket, byte[] body) {
   925	        String xml = new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
   926	        String mode = XmlParser.extractFirst(xml, "Mode", null);
   927	        String daysStr = XmlParser.extractFirst(xml, "Days", null);
   928	        String yearsStr = XmlParser.extractFirst(xml, "Years", null);
   929	        String unit = null;
   930	        int value = 0;
   931	        if (daysStr != null) {
   932	            unit = "Days";
   933	            value = Integer.parseInt(daysStr);
   934	        } else if (yearsStr != null) {
   935	            unit = "Years";
   936	            value = Integer.parseInt(yearsStr);
   937	        }
   938	        s3Service.putObjectLockConfiguration(bucket, mode, unit, value);
   939	        return Response.ok().build();
   940	    }
   941	
   942	    private Response handleGetObjectLockConfiguration(String bucket) {
   943	        ObjectLockRetention retention =
   944	                s3Service.getObjectLockConfiguration(bucket);
   945	        XmlBuilder xml = new XmlBuilder()
   946	                .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
   947	                .start("ObjectLockConfiguration", AwsNamespaces.S3)
   948	                .elem("ObjectLockEnabled", "Enabled");
   949	        if (retention != null) {
   950	            xml.start("Rule").start("DefaultRetention")
   951	               .elem("Mode", retention.mode());
   952	            if ("Days".equals(retention.unit())) {
   953	                xml.elem("Days", retention.value());
   954	            } else {
   955	                xml.elem("Years", retention.value());
   956	            }
   957	            xml.end("DefaultRetention").end("Rule");
   958	        }
   959	        xml.end("ObjectLockConfiguration");
   960	        return Response.ok(xml.build()).type(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML).build();
   961	    }

   963	    // --- Object Retention ---
   964	
   965	    private Response handlePutObjectRetention(String bucket, String key, String versionId,
   966	                                               HttpHeaders httpHeaders, byte[] body) {
   967	        String xml = new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
   968	        String mode = XmlParser.extractFirst(xml, "Mode", null);
   969	        String dateStr = XmlParser.extractFirst(xml, "RetainUntilDate", null);
   970	        Instant retainUntil = dateStr != null ? Instant.parse(dateStr) : null;
   971	        boolean bypass = "true".equalsIgnoreCase(
   972	                httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-bypass-governance-retention"));
   973	        s3Service.putObjectRetention(bucket, key, versionId, mode, retainUntil, bypass);
   974	        return Response.ok().build();
   975	    }
   976	
   977	    private Response handleGetObjectRetention(String bucket, String key, String versionId) {
   978	        S3Object obj = s3Service.getObjectRetention(bucket, key, versionId);
   979	        XmlBuilder xml = new XmlBuilder()
   980	                .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
   981	                .start("Retention", AwsNamespaces.S3)
   982	                .elem("Mode", obj.getObjectLockMode());
   983	        if (obj.getRetainUntilDate() != null) {
   984	            xml.elem("RetainUntilDate", ISO_FORMAT.format(obj.getRetainUntilDate()));
   985	        }
   986	        xml.end("Retention");
   987	        return Response.ok(xml.build()).type(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML).build();
   988	    }

  1008	                .start("LegalHold", AwsNamespaces.S3)

  1014	
  1015	    private void appendObjectHeaders(Response.ResponseBuilder resp, S3Object obj) {
  1016	        if (obj.getStorageClass() != null) {
  1017	            resp.header("x-amz-storage-class", obj.getStorageClass());
  1018	        }
  1019	        if (obj.getMetadata() != null) {
  1020	            for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : obj.getMetadata().entrySet()) {
  1021	                resp.header("x-amz-meta-" + entry.getKey(), entry.getValue());
  1022	            }
  1023	        }
  1024	        appendChecksumHeaders(resp, obj.getChecksum());
  1025	        appendLockHeaders(resp, obj);
  1026	    }
  1027	
  1028	    private void appendLockHeaders(Response.ResponseBuilder resp, S3Object obj) {
  1029	        if (obj.getObjectLockMode() != null) {
  1030	            resp.header("x-amz-object-lock-mode", obj.getObjectLockMode());
  1031	        }
  1032	        if (obj.getRetainUntilDate() != null) {
  1033	            resp.header("x-amz-object-lock-retain-until-date",
  1034	                    DateTimeFormatter.ISO_INSTANT.format(obj.getRetainUntilDate()));
  1035	        }
  1036	        if (obj.getLegalHoldStatus() != null) {
  1037	            resp.header("x-amz-object-lock-legal-hold", obj.getLegalHoldStatus());
  1038	        }
  1039	    }
  1040	
  1041	    // --- Helpers ---
  1042	
  1043	    private Response handleCopyObject(String copySource, String destBucket, String destKey,
  1044	                                      String contentType, HttpHeaders httpHeaders) {
  1045	        String source = copySource.startsWith("/") ? copySource.substring(1) : copySource;
  1046	        int slashIndex = source.indexOf('/');
  1047	        if (slashIndex < 0) {
  1048	            throw new AwsException("InvalidArgument", "Invalid copy source: " + copySource, 400);
  1049	        }
  1050	        String sourceBucket = source.substring(0, slashIndex);
  1051	        String sourceKey = source.substring(slashIndex + 1);
  1052	
  1053	        S3Object copy = s3Service.copyObject(sourceBucket, sourceKey, destBucket, destKey,
  1054	                httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-metadata-directive"),
  1055	                extractUserMetadata(httpHeaders),
  1056	                httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-storage-class"),
  1057	                contentType);
  1058	        String xml = new XmlBuilder()
  1059	                .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
  1060	                .start("CopyObjectResult", AwsNamespaces.S3)
  1061	                .elem("LastModified", ISO_FORMAT.format(copy.getLastModified()))
  1062	                .elem("ETag", copy.getETag())
  1063	                .end("CopyObjectResult")
  1064	                .build();
  1065	        return Response.ok(xml).build();
  1066	    }
  1067	
  1068	    private Response handleGetObjectAttributes(String bucket, String key, String versionId,
  1069	                                               String objectAttributesHeader, Integer maxParts,
  1070	                                               Integer partNumberMarker) {
  1071	        Set<ObjectAttributeName> attributes = ObjectAttributeName.parseHeader(objectAttributesHeader);
  1072	        GetObjectAttributesResult result = s3Service.getObjectAttributes(bucket, key, versionId,
  1073	                attributes, maxParts, partNumberMarker);
  1074	
  1075	        XmlBuilder xml = new XmlBuilder()
  1076	                .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
  1077	                .start("GetObjectAttributesResponse", AwsNamespaces.S3)
  1078	                .elem("ETag", result.getETag());
  1079	        appendChecksum(xml, result.getChecksum());
  1080	        appendObjectParts(xml, result.getObjectParts());
  1081	        if (result.getStorageClass() != null) {
  1082	            xml.elem("StorageClass", result.getStorageClass());
  1083	        }
  1084	        if (result.getObjectSize() != null) {
  1085	            xml.elem("ObjectSize", result.getObjectSize());
  1086	        }
  1087	        xml.end("GetObjectAttributesResponse");
  1088	
  1089	        Response.ResponseBuilder response = Response.ok(xml.build()).type(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML);
  1090	        if (result.getLastModified() != null) {
  1091	            response.header("Last-Modified", RFC_822.format(result.getLastModified()));
  1092	        }
  1093	        if (result.getVersionId() != null) {
  1094	            response.header("x-amz-version-id", result.getVersionId());
  1095	        }
  1096	        return response.build();
  1097	    }
  1098	
  1099	    private void appendChecksum(XmlBuilder xml, S3Checksum checksum) {
  1100	        if (checksum == null || !checksum.hasAnyValue()) {
  1101	            return;
  1102	        }
  1103	        xml.start("Checksum")
  1104	                .elem("ChecksumCRC32", checksum.getChecksumCRC32())
  1105	                .elem("ChecksumCRC32C", checksum.getChecksumCRC32C())
  1106	                .elem("ChecksumCRC64NVME", checksum.getChecksumCRC64NVME())
  1107	                .elem("ChecksumSHA1", checksum.getChecksumSHA1())
  1108	                .elem("ChecksumSHA256", checksum.getChecksumSHA256())
  1109	                .elem("ChecksumType", checksum.getChecksumType())
  1110	                .end("Checksum");
  1111	    }
  1112	
  1113	    private void appendObjectParts(XmlBuilder xml, GetObjectAttributesParts objectParts) {
  1114	        if (objectParts == null) {
  1115	            return;
  1116	        }
  1117	        xml.start("ObjectParts")
  1118	                .elem("IsTruncated", objectParts.isTruncated())
  1119	                .elem("MaxParts", objectParts.getMaxParts())
  1120	                .elem("NextPartNumberMarker", objectParts.getNextPartNumberMarker())
  1121	                .elem("PartNumberMarker", objectParts.getPartNumberMarker());
  1122	        for (Part part : objectParts.getParts()) {
  1123	            xml.start("Part")
  1124	                    .elem("ChecksumCRC32", part.getChecksum().getChecksumCRC32())
  1125	                    .elem("ChecksumCRC32C", part.getChecksum().getChecksumCRC32C())
  1126	                    .elem("ChecksumCRC64NVME", part.getChecksum().getChecksumCRC64NVME())
  1127	                    .elem("ChecksumSHA1", part.getChecksum().getChecksumSHA1())
  1128	                    .elem("ChecksumSHA256", part.getChecksum().getChecksumSHA256())
  1129	                    .elem("PartNumber", part.getPartNumber())
  1130	                    .elem("Size", part.getSize())
  1131	                    .end("Part");
  1132	        }
  1133	        xml.elem("PartsCount", objectParts.getPartsCount())
  1134	                .end("ObjectParts");
  1135	    }
  1136	
  1137	    private void appendChecksumHeaders(Response.ResponseBuilder resp, S3Checksum checksum) {
  1138	        if (checksum == null) {
  1139	            return;
  1140	        }
  1141	        if (checksum.getChecksumSHA1() != null) {
  1142	            resp.header("x-amz-checksum-sha1", checksum.getChecksumSHA1());
  1143	        }
  1144	        if (checksum.getChecksumSHA256() != null) {
  1145	            resp.header("x-amz-checksum-sha256", checksum.getChecksumSHA256());
  1146	        }
  1147	    }
  1148	
  1149	    private Map<String, String> extractUserMetadata(HttpHeaders httpHeaders) {
  1150	        Map<String, String> metadata = new LinkedHashMap<>();
  1151	        for (Map.Entry<String, List<String>> entry : httpHeaders.getRequestHeaders().entrySet()) {
  1152	            String headerName = entry.getKey().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  1153	            if (!headerName.startsWith("x-amz-meta-")) {
  1154	                continue;
  1155	            }
  1156	            String key = headerName.substring("x-amz-meta-".length());
  1157	            if (!key.isBlank() && !entry.getValue().isEmpty()) {
  1158	                metadata.put(key, entry.getValue().get(0));
  1159	            }
  1160	        }
  1161	        return metadata;
  1162	    }
  1163	
  1164	    private void validateChecksumHeaders(HttpHeaders httpHeaders, byte[] data) {
  1165	        String sha1 = httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-checksum-sha1");
  1166	        if (sha1 != null && !sha1.equals(S3Checksum.sha1Base64(data))) {
  1167	            throw new AwsException("BadDigest", "The SHA1 checksum you specified did not match the payload.", 400);
  1168	        }
  1169	
  1170	        String sha256 = httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-checksum-sha256");
  1171	        if (sha256 != null && !sha256.equals(S3Checksum.sha256Base64(data))) {
  1172	            throw new AwsException("BadDigest", "The SHA256 checksum you specified did not match the payload.", 400);
  1173	        }
  1174	    }
  1175	
  1176	    private Response xmlErrorResponse(AwsException e) {
  1177	        String xml = new XmlBuilder()
  1178	                .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
  1179	                .start("Error")
  1180	                .elem("Code", e.getErrorCode())
  1181	                .elem("Message", e.getMessage())
  1182	                .elem("RequestId", java.util.UUID.randomUUID().toString())
  1183	                .end("Error")
  1184	                .build();
  1185	        return Response.status(e.getHttpStatus()).entity(xml).type(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML).build();
  1186	    }
  1187	
  1188	    private Response checkPreconditions(S3Object obj, String ifMatch, String ifNoneMatch,
  1189	                                         String ifModifiedSince, String ifUnmodifiedSince) {
  1190	        String eTag = obj.getETag();
  1191	        Instant lastModified = obj.getLastModified();
  1192	
  1193	        if (ifMatch != null && !eTagMatches(ifMatch, eTag)) {
  1194	            return preconditionFailedResponse();
  1195	        }
  1196	
  1197	        if (ifUnmodifiedSince != null && ifMatch == null) {
  1198	            Instant since = parseHttpDate(ifUnmodifiedSince);
  1199	            if (since != null && lastModified.isAfter(since)) {
  1200	                return preconditionFailedResponse();
  1201	            }
  1202	        }
  1203	
  1204	        if (ifNoneMatch != null && eTagMatches(ifNoneMatch, eTag)) {
  1205	            return notModifiedResponse(eTag, lastModified);
  1206	        }
  1207	
  1208	        if (ifModifiedSince != null && ifNoneMatch == null) {
  1209	            Instant since = parseHttpDate(ifModifiedSince);
  1210	            if (since != null && !lastModified.isAfter(since)) {
  1211	                return notModifiedResponse(eTag, lastModified);
  1212	            }
  1213	        }
  1214	
  1215	        return null;
  1216	    }
  1217	
  1218	    private boolean hasPreconditions(String ifMatch, String ifNoneMatch,
  1219	                                      String ifModifiedSince, String ifUnmodifiedSince) {
  1220	        return ifMatch != null || ifNoneMatch != null || ifModifiedSince != null || ifUnmodifiedSince != null;
  1221	    }
  1222	
  1223	    private Response notModifiedResponse(String eTag, Instant lastModified) {
  1224	        return Response.notModified()
  1225	                .header("ETag", eTag)
  1226	                .header("Last-Modified", RFC_822.format(lastModified))
  1227	                .build();
  1228	    }
  1229	
  1230	    private Response preconditionFailedResponse() {
  1231	        return xmlErrorResponse(new AwsException("PreconditionFailed",
  1232	                "At least one of the pre-conditions you specified did not hold.", 412));
  1233	    }
  1234	
  1235	    private boolean eTagMatches(String headerValue, String eTag) {
  1236	        if ("*".equals(headerValue.trim())) {
  1237	            return true;
  1238	        }
  1239	        for (String candidate : headerValue.split(",")) {
  1240	            if (candidate.trim().equals(eTag)) {
  1241	                return true;
  1242	            }
  1243	        }
  1244	        return false;
  1245	    }
  1246	
  1247	    private Instant parseHttpDate(String dateStr) {
  1248	        try {
  1249	            return RFC_822.parse(dateStr.trim(), Instant::from);
  1250	        } catch (Exception e) {
  1251	            try {
  1252	                return Instant.parse(dateStr.trim());
  1253	            } catch (Exception e2) {
  1254	                return null;
  1255	            }
  1256	        }
  1257	    }
  1258	
  1259	    private boolean hasQueryParam(UriInfo uriInfo, String param) {
  1260	        if (uriInfo.getQueryParameters().containsKey(param)) return true;
  1261	        String query = uriInfo.getRequestUri().getQuery();
  1262	        if (query == null) return false;
  1263	        return query.equals(param) || query.contains(param + "&") || query.contains("&" + param);
  1264	    }
  1265	}

The issue is clear: in the `handleCopyObject` method, the `sourceKey` from the `x-amz-copy-source` header may be percent-encoded (e.g., `src/%E3%83%86%E3%82%B9%E3%83%88%E7%94%BB%E5%83%8F.png`), and it's not being URL-decoded before being passed to `s3Service.copyObject()`.

2026-05-30 03:51:40,869 - INFO - swea-agent-floci-io__floci-112 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I have a clear picture. Let me trace the problem:

1. When a client sends a `PUT` request with `x-amz-copy-source: /test-bucket/src/%E3%83%86%E3%82%B9%E3%83%88%E7%94%BB%E5%83%8F.png`, the `copySource` parameter in `S3Controller.putObject()` receives the raw value (percent-encoded).

2. In `handleCopyObject()`, the code does:
```java
String source = copySource.startsWith("/") ? copySource.substring(1) : copySource;
int slashIndex = source.indexOf('/');
String sourceBucket = source.substring(0, slashIndex);
String sourceKey = source.substring(slashIndex + 1);  // This is still percent-encoded!
```

3. Then `s3Service.copyObject(sourceBucket, sourceKey, ...)` is called with the percent-encoded key, which doesn't match the actual stored key (which was URL-decoded when received as a path parameter).

The path parameter `@PathParam("key")` is automatically URL-decoded by JAX-RS, so the key stored is the decoded version (e.g., `src/テスト画像.png`). But the `x-amz-copy-source` header value is NOT URL-decoded.

The fix should be to URL-decode the source key in `handleCopyObject`. Let me implement this.



🎬 ACTION

2026-05-30 03:51:59,841 - INFO - swea-agent-floci-io__floci-112 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now let me also check if the `copySource` could have a versionId appended with `?versionId=xxx`. In AWS S3, the `x-amz-copy-source` header can optionally include a version ID like `/bucket/key?versionId=xxx`. Let me check how that's handled:

Looking at the current code, it doesn't handle `?versionId=` at all. But that's a separate issue. The immediate bug is about URL encoding.

Let me now also think about edge cases:

1. The source key might contain `+` signs, which in URL encoding represent spaces. `URLDecoder.decode` will convert `+` to space, which is correct for query strings but might be wrong for path segments. However, AWS S3 uses percent-encoding for the `x-amz-copy-source` header, where `%20` is used for spaces, not `+`. So `URLDecoder.decode` should be fine here.

2. The source key might already be unencoded (ASCII-only keys). `URLDecoder.decode` on an already-decoded string like `greeting.txt` returns `greeting.txt` unchanged.

3. The source key might have `?versionId=...` appended. Let me check if this is handled. Looking at the current code, it doesn't handle versionId in the copy source at all. But that's beyond the scope of this bug.

Let me also consider: what about the source bucket? Can bucket names contain non-ASCII characters? AWS S3 bucket names must be DNS-compliant (ASCII only), so bucket names should never need URL decoding. So we only need to decode the key.

Now let me also check if there's a similar issue elsewhere - perhaps the `copySource` could also come with versionId in the query string. Let me handle that too, since the `?versionId=...` part (if present) should NOT be decoded as part of the key name. Actually, looking at the AWS documentation, the `x-amz-copy-source` header should be URL-encoded, and the key path should be decoded. The `?versionId=xxx` is part of the URL query string and should be handled separately.

Let me look at what the AWS SDK sends in the copy-source header. The format is typically:
`/bucket-name/key-name` or `/bucket-name/key-name?versionId=xxx`

The current code doesn't handle `?versionId=` at all. But that's a separate pre-existing issue. Let me focus on the URL decoding fix.

Wait, I should also check that the destination key is already URL-decoded by JAX-RS (since it comes as a path parameter). Let me verify this is the case:

The `@PathParam("key")` in the `putObject` method will indeed be URL-decoded by JAX-RS. So the destination key is fine. Only the source key from the header needs decoding.

Let me now run the test suite to make sure my changes work

                                      String contentType, HttpHeaders httpHeaders) {
        String source = copySource.startsWith("/") ? copySource.substring(1) : copySource;
        int slashIndex = source.indexOf('"'"'/'"'"');
        if (slashIndex < 0) {
            throw new AwsException("InvalidArgument", "Invalid copy source: " + copySource, 400);
        }
        String sourceBucket = source.substring(0, slashIndex);
        String rawKey = source.substring(slashIndex + 1);
        // Remove ?versionId= suffix if present (AWS S3 expects the versionId to be in the query string)
        int queryIndex = rawKey.indexOf('"'"'?'"'"');
        String versionId = null;
        if (queryIndex >= 0) {
            String query = rawKey.substring(queryIndex + 1);
            rawKey = rawKey.substring(0, queryIndex);
            // Parse versionId from query string
            for (String param : query.split("&")) {
                if (param.startsWith("versionId=")) {
                    versionId = param.substring("versionId=".length());
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
        // URL-decode the key: AWS SDKs percent-encode non-ASCII characters in the x-amz-copy-source header
        String sourceKey;
        try {
            sourceKey = URLDecoder.decode(rawKey, StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
        } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {
            // If the key contains invalid percent sequences, use it as-is
            sourceKey = rawKey;
        }'

  1045	                                      String contentType, HttpHeaders httpHeaders) {
  1046	        String source = copySource.startsWith("/") ? copySource.substring(1) : copySource;
  1047	        int slashIndex = source.indexOf('/');
  1048	        if (slashIndex < 0) {
  1049	            throw new AwsException("InvalidArgument", "Invalid copy source: " + copySource, 400);
  1050	        }
  1051	        String sourceBucket = source.substring(0, slashIndex);
  1052	        String sourceKey = source.substring(slashIndex + 1);
  1053

  1055	                httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-metadata-directive"),
  1056	                extractUserMetadata(httpHeaders),
  1057	                httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-storage-class"),
  1058	                contentType);

  1063	                .elem("ETag", copy.getETag())
  1064	                .end("CopyObjectResult")
  1065	                .build();
  1066	        return Response.ok(xml).build();
  1067	    }

cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/patch.py << 'PYEOF'
import re

with open('src/main/java/io/github/hectorvent/floci/services/s3/S3Controller.java', 'r') as f:
    content = f.read()

old = '''    private Response handleCopyObject(String copySource, String destBucket, String destKey,
                                      String contentType, HttpHeaders httpHeaders) {
        String source = copySource.startsWith("/") ? copySource.substring(1) : copySource;
        int slashIndex = source.indexOf('/');
        if (slashIndex < 0) {
            throw new AwsException("InvalidArgument", "Invalid copy source: " + copySource, 400);
        }
        String sourceBucket = source.substring(0, slashIndex);
        String sourceKey = source.substring(slashIndex + 1);

        S3Object copy = s3Service.copyObject(sourceBucket, sourceKey, destBucket, destKey,
                httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-metadata-directive"),
                extractUserMetadata(httpHeaders),
                httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-storage-class"),
                contentType);'''

new = '''    private Response handleCopyObject(String copySource, String destBucket, String destKey,
                                      String contentType, HttpHeaders httpHeaders) {
        String source = copySource.startsWith("/") ? copySource.substring(1) : copySource;
        int slashIndex = source.indexOf('/');
        if (slashIndex < 0) {
            throw new AwsException("InvalidArgument", "Invalid copy source: " + copySource, 400);
        }
        String sourceBucket = source.substring(0, slashIndex);
        String rawKey = source.substring(slashIndex + 1);
        // Remove ?versionId= suffix if present (AWS S3 expects the versionId to be in the query string)
        int queryIndex = rawKey.indexOf('?');
        String versionId = null;
        if (queryIndex >= 0) {
            String query = rawKey.substring(queryIndex + 1);
            rawKey = rawKey.substring(0, queryIndex);
            // Parse versionId from query string
            for (String param : query.split("&")) {
                if (param.startsWith("versionId=")) {
                    versionId = param.substring("versionId=".length());
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
        // URL-decode the key: AWS SDKs percent-encode non-ASCII characters in the x-amz-copy-source header
        String sourceKey;
        try {
            sourceKey = URLDecoder.decode(rawKey, StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
        } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {
            // If the key contains invalid percent sequences, use it as-is
            sourceKey = rawKey;
        }

        S3Object copy = s3Service.copyObject(sourceBucket, sourceKey, destBucket, destKey,
                httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-metadata-directive"),
                extractUserMetadata(httpHeaders),
                httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-storage-class"),
                contentType);'''

assert old in content, "Old string not found!"
content = content.replace(old, new)

with open('src/main/java/io/github/hectorvent/floci/services/s3/S3Controller.java', 'w') as f:
    f.write(content)

print("Done!")
PYEOF

This meant it was looking up an object with the literal key `src/%E3%83%86%E3%82%B9%E3%83%88%E7%94%BB%E5%83%8F.png` instead of `src/テスト画像.png`, resulting in `NoSuchKey`.\n\nMeanwhile, `PutObject` and `GetObject` worked correctly because the key comes as a `@PathParam` which JAX-RS automatically URL-decodes.\n\n### Fix\n\nModified `handleCopyObject` in `S3Controller.java` to:\n\n1. **URL-decode the source key** using `URLDecoder.decode(rawKey, StandardCharsets.UTF_8)` - this properly converts percent-encoded UTF-8 sequences back to the original characters.\n\n2. **Handle `versionId` query parameter** in the copy source (e.g., `/bucket/key?versionId=xxx`) - parse and remove it before URL-decoding the key.\n\n3. **Gracefully handle invalid percent sequences** - if `URLDecoder.decode` throws `IllegalArgumentException`, fall back to using the raw key as-is.', role='assistant', tool_calls=None, function_call=None, provider_specific_fields={'refusal': None}), provider_specific_fields={'content_filter_results': {}})], usage=Usage(completion_tokens=402, prompt_tokens=66872, total_tokens=67274, completion_tokens_details=None, prompt_tokens_details=None, audio_prompt_tokens=0), service_tier=None, prompt_filter_results=None)

  1044	    private Response handleCopyObject(String copySource, String destBucket, String destKey,
  1045	                                      String contentType, HttpHeaders httpHeaders) {
  1046	        String source = copySource.startsWith("/") ? copySource.substring(1) : copySource;
  1047	        int slashIndex = source.indexOf('/');
  1048	        if (slashIndex < 0) {
  1049	            throw new AwsException("InvalidArgument", "Invalid copy source: " + copySource, 400);
  1050	        }
  1051	        String sourceBucket = source.substring(0, slashIndex);
  1052	        String rawKey = source.substring(slashIndex + 1);
  1053	        // Remove ?versionId= suffix if present (AWS S3 expects the versionId to be in the query string)
  1054	        int queryIndex = rawKey.indexOf('?');
  1055	        String versionId = null;
  1056	        if (queryIndex >= 0) {
  1057	            String query = rawKey.substring(queryIndex + 1);
  1058	            rawKey = rawKey.substring(0, queryIndex);
  1059	            // Parse versionId from query string
  1060	            for (String param : query.split("&")) {
  1061	                if (param.startsWith("versionId=")) {
  1062	                    versionId = param.substring("versionId=".length());
  1063	                    break;
  1064	                }
  1065	            }
  1066	        }
  1067	        // URL-decode the key: AWS SDKs percent-encode non-ASCII characters in the x-amz-copy-source header
  1068	        String sourceKey;
  1069	        try {
  1070	            sourceKey = URLDecoder.decode(rawKey, StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
  1071	        } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {
  1072	            // If the key contains invalid percent sequences, use it as-is
  1073	            sourceKey = rawKey;
  1074	        }
  1075	
  1076	        S3Object copy = s3Service.copyObject(sourceBucket, sourceKey, destBucket, destKey,
  1077	                httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-metadata-directive"),
  1078	                extractUserMetadata(httpHeaders),
  1079	                httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-storage-class"),
  1080	                contentType);
  1081	        String xml = new XmlBuilder()
  1082	                .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
  1083	                .start("CopyObjectResult", AwsNamespaces.S3)
  1084	                .elem("LastModified", ISO_FORMAT.format(copy.getLastModified()))
  1085	                .elem("ETag", copy.getETag())
  1086	                .end("CopyObjectResult")
  1087	                .build();
  1088	        return Response.ok(xml).build();
  1089	    }
